Pending control and the remaining VM/native boundary templates remain later 07-S5 work.

The source-contract suite now also locks legacy int arithmetic direct lowering. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_legacy_int_arithmetic_to_direct_c_expressions` first failed on missing `zr_aot_arith_exec_int`, then passed after `ADD_INT`, `ADD_INT_CONST`, `SUB_INT`, and `SUB_INT_CONST` moved into `backend_aot_c_lowering_legacy_int_arithmetic.c`. The contract requires the direct stack/stack and stack/constant `+` / `-` expression shapes, the shared integer-like constant literal formatter, function-body routing for both const and non-const int opcodes, explicit unsupported const failures, and absence of generated-C `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_AddIntConst`, `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_SubInt`, and `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_SubIntConst` calls in that lowering module.

The source-contract suite now locks generic numeric arithmetic boundary-helper lowering. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_generic_numeric_arithmetic_to_boundary_helpers` first failed after requiring `zr_aot_arith_exec_generic_numeric_binary_boundary` and the `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_GenericNumeric*()` helper family while the generator still expanded direct tag branches. It passed after generic `ADD`, `SUB`, `MUL`, `DIV`, `MOD`, and `NEG` moved to helper guards and the numeric primitive branches moved into `aot_runtime_values.c`. The contract requires emitter declarations and function-body routing for those opcodes, generated boundary markers and helper calls, runtime helper declarations and implementations, preservation of `divide by zero`, `modulo by zero`, and `fmod(leftFloat, rightFloat)` semantics, and absence of old generated numeric extraction helpers, direct `ZrCore_Stack_GetValue(frame.slotBase + %u)` locals, generated tag ladders, direct expression strings, and generated unary negation templates.

The source-contract suite now also locks generic primitive conversion boundary-helper lowering. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_generic_primitive_conversions_to_boundary_helpers` first failed after requiring helper-only generic primitive conversion lowering, then passed after generic `TO_BOOL`, `TO_INT`, `TO_UINT`, and `TO_FLOAT` moved onto dedicated `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_ConvertGenericTo*()` helpers. The contract requires conversion markers and helper guards in generated C, helper declarations and implementations in the AOT runtime, and absence of generated direct conversion stack locals, tag-branch templates, generated unsupported conversion blocks, or broader `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_To*()` helper reuse from the generated lowering path.

The AOT C source-contract suite now has a separate logical contract target so the older source-contract file does not keep growing past its current large-file boundary. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_generic_truthiness_to_boundary_helpers` first failed after requiring helper-only generic primitive truthiness lowering, then passed after generic `LOGICAL_NOT` and `JUMP_IF` moved onto dedicated `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_GenericPrimitiveLogicalNot()` and `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_GenericPrimitiveIsTruthy()` helpers. The 2026-06-22 local-sync tightening then required `zr_aot_generic_logical_sync_bool_local_boundary` and `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_SyncBoolLocal()` for helper-written bool destinations, forbidding the old generated `zr_aot_bool_sync` slot lookup and payload reload. The contract requires generated markers, helper guards, bool scalar-local sync after helper-written `LOGICAL_NOT` destinations, runtime primitive truthiness helper coverage, and absence of old generated primitive truthiness branch templates or broader `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_LogicalNot` / `IsTruthy` calls from the generic logical lowering path.

The logical source-contract suite now also locks generic primitive equality boundary-helper lowering. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_generic_primitive_equality_to_boundary_helpers` first failed after requiring helper-only generic primitive equality lowering, then passed after generic `LOGICAL_EQUAL` and `LOGICAL_NOT_EQUAL` moved onto dedicated `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_GenericPrimitiveLogicalEqual()` and `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_GenericPrimitiveLogicalNotEqual()` helpers. The 2026-06-22 local-sync tightening also makes equality/inequality bool scalar-local refresh helper-owned via `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_SyncBoolLocal()`, so generated C no longer emits `const SZrTypeValue *zr_aot_bool_sync = ZrCore_Stack_GetValue(frame.slotBase + slot)`. The contract requires generated markers, helper guards, bool scalar-local sync after helper-written destinations, runtime primitive equality helper coverage, and absence of old generated same-type/equality branch templates, generated unsupported equality blocks, `ZrCore_Value_Equal`, or broader `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_LogicalEqual` / `LogicalNotEqual` calls from the generic logical lowering path.

The logical source-contract suite now also locks bool binary logical direct lowering. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_bool_logical_and_or_to_direct_c` first failed on missing `backend_aot_write_c_direct_logical_and`, then passed after `LOGICAL_AND` and `LOGICAL_OR` were routed through direct generated-C emitters in `backend_aot_c_lowering_generic_logical.c`. The contract requires bool operand validation, normalized bool payload reads, direct `&&` / `||` C expressions, direct bool destination writes, explicit unsupported non-bool failures, function-body routing for both opcodes, and absence of generated-C `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_LogicalAnd` / `LogicalOr` calls from the logical module and dispatcher path.

The logical source-contract suite now also locks typed string equality direct lowering. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_string_equality_to_direct_c` first failed on missing `backend_aot_write_c_direct_logical_equal_string`, then passed after `LOGICAL_EQUAL_STRING` and `LOGICAL_NOT_EQUAL_STRING` were routed through direct generated-C emitters in `backend_aot_c_lowering_generic_logical.c`. The contract requires generated module includes for `zr_vm_core/string.h` and `<string.h>`, string operand validation, `ZR_CAST_STRING`, byte-length and native-byte accessors, direct `memcmp(...) == 0`, direct bool destination writes, explicit unsupported string equality failures, function-body routing for both opcodes, and absence of generated-C `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_LogicalEqualString` / `LogicalNotEqualString` / `ZrCore_String_Equal` calls from the C lowering path.

The shift source-contract suite now locks generic integer shift direct lowering. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_generic_integer_shift_to_direct_c` first failed on missing generic shift direct emitter declarations, then passed after generic `SHIFT_LEFT` and `SHIFT_RIGHT` moved from `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_ShiftLeft` / `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_ShiftRight` helper calls to direct generated-C emitters in `backend_aot_c_lowering_typed_bitwise.c`. The contract requires integer operand validation, direct `<<` and `>>` expression shapes, shift-count guards, direct `ZR_VALUE_FAST_SET` result writes, explicit unsupported generic integer shift failures, function-body routing for both opcodes, and absence of generated-C generic shift runtime helper calls from the C lowering path.

The float source-contract suite now locks typed float modulo direct lowering. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_typed_float_mod_to_direct_c` first failed because `backend_aot_c_lowering_typed_float_mod.c` did not exist, then passed after `MOD_FLOAT` moved from `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_ModFloat(state, &frame, ...)` to a direct generated-C `fmod` emitter. The contract requires the new emitter declaration, generated module `#include <math.h>`, float operand validation, direct `fmod(zr_aot_left_scalar, zr_aot_right_scalar)`, a `modulo by zero` guard, direct `ZR_VALUE_FAST_SET` result writes, function-body routing for `MOD_FLOAT`, and absence of the old `ModFloat` helper route from the C lowering path.

The generic numeric source-contract suite now locks generic `MOD` float fallback through the same boundary helper. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_generic_numeric_mod_float_fallback_to_boundary_helper` requires generated C to call `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_GenericNumericMod(state, &frame, %u, %u, %u)` while `aot_runtime_values.c` owns `<math.h>`, `modulo by zero`, and `fmod(leftFloat, rightFloat)`. The contract rejects the old generated float branch, shared zero-guard emitter, direct `fmod(zr_aot_left_float, zr_aot_right_float)`, direct `ZR_VALUE_TYPE_DOUBLE` write, and signed/unsigned direct `%` expression templates from the C lowering module.

The power source-contract suite now locks typed power direct lowering. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_typed_power_to_direct_c` first failed because `backend_aot_c_lowering_typed_power.c` did not exist, then passed after `POW_SIGNED`, `POW_UNSIGNED`, and `POW_FLOAT` moved from typed power runtime helper calls to direct generated-C emitters. The contract requires direct emitter declarations, signed/unsigned/float operand validation, `power domain error`, integer exponentiation-by-squaring loop markers, direct `pow(zr_aot_left_scalar, zr_aot_right_scalar)`, direct `ZR_VALUE_FAST_SET` result writes, function-body routing for the three typed opcodes, and absence of the old typed power helper routes from the C lowering path.

The same source-contract suite now also checks signed load-const arithmetic as a separate module boundary. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_typed_signed_load_const_arithmetic_to_c_expressions` first failed because `backend_aot_c_lowering_typed_arithmetic_load_const.c` did not exist, then passed after the module was added and `ADD_SIGNED_LOAD_CONST`, `SUB_SIGNED_LOAD_CONST`, `MUL_SIGNED_LOAD_CONST`, `DIV_SIGNED_LOAD_CONST`, and `MOD_SIGNED_LOAD_CONST` were routed through direct C emitters. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_typed_signed_load_stack_const_arithmetic_to_c_expressions` first failed on missing stack-const emitter declarations, then passed after the same module added direct lowering for `ADD_SIGNED_LOAD_STACK_CONST`, `SUB_SIGNED_LOAD_STACK_CONST`, `MUL_SIGNED_LOAD_STACK_CONST`, `DIV_SIGNED_LOAD_STACK_CONST`, and `MOD_SIGNED_LOAD_STACK_CONST`. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_typed_signed_load_stack_load_const_arithmetic_to_c_expressions` first failed on missing `backend_aot_write_c_direct_add_signed_load_stack_load_const`, then passed after `ADD_SIGNED_LOAD_STACK_LOAD_CONST` was routed through direct materialization and C `+` lowering. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_typed_signed_load_stack_arithmetic_to_c_expressions` first failed because `backend_aot_c_lowering_typed_arithmetic_load_stack.c` was missing, then passed after `ADD_SIGNED_LOAD_STACK` was routed through direct stack/stack C `+` lowering; it later failed on missing `zr_aot_left_scalar * zr_aot_right_scalar`, then passed after `MUL_SIGNED_LOAD_STACK` joined the same direct stack/stack lowering module with an `INT64` result tag. The contracts lock constant and stack-source materialization, direct `+`, `-`, `*`, `/`, `%` expressions, divide/modulo zero guards, function-body routing, and executable-subset support for these signed quickening families.

The same test now locks typed signed/unsigned `%` lowering: direct emitter declarations, `zr_aot_left_scalar % zr_aot_right_scalar`, `zr_aot_left_scalar % zr_aot_right_literal`, `ADD_SIGNED_MOD_CONST`'s direct add-plus-mod expression, `modulo by zero`, function-body routing for typed modulo opcodes, and absence of direct signed/unsigned modulo helper strings for those opcode families. It also locks typed numeric comparison lowering: signed/unsigned/float comparison emitter declarations, `zr_aot_compare_exec_*` source markers, `==`, `!=`, `>`, `<`, `>=`, and `<=` scalar expressions, function-body routing for typed numeric comparison opcodes, and absence of direct `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_Logical*` helper strings for those opcode families.

The bitwise source-contract test `test_aot_c_source_lowers_typed_bitwise_to_c_expressions` locks the separate typed bitwise lowering module, emitter declarations, C expression shapes for `~`, `&`, `|`, `^`, signed shift-right, unsigned left/right shift intermediates, shift-count range checks, function-body routing for typed bitwise and shift opcodes, and absence of direct bitwise/typed-shift runtime helper strings for those opcode families.

The bool logical source-contract test `test_aot_c_source_lowers_typed_bool_equality_to_c_expressions` locks the separate typed logical lowering module, bool equality and logical-not emitter declarations, `zr_aot_bool_compare_exec` / `zr_aot_bool_not_exec` source markers, direct `==` / `!=` / `!` bool expressions, function-body routing for `LOGICAL_EQUAL_BOOL` / `LOGICAL_NOT_EQUAL_BOOL` / `LOGICAL_NOT_BOOL`, typed bool false-branch routing for `JUMP_IF_BOOL_FALSE`, `zr_aot_jump_if_bool_false`, and absence of direct bool equality/logical-not runtime helper strings for those proven-bool opcode families.

The signed branch source-contract test `test_aot_c_source_lowers_typed_signed_branch_to_c_comparisons` locks the fused signed branch family. It requires direct emitter declarations for `JUMP_IF_GREATER_SIGNED`, `JUMP_IF_LESS_EQUAL_SIGNED`, `JUMP_IF_NOT_EQUAL_SIGNED`, and `JUMP_IF_NOT_EQUAL_SIGNED_CONST`; direct generated C comparison expressions for `>`, `<=`, slot/slot `!=`, and slot/constant `!=`; function-body routing; executable-subset support; AotExecIR conditional-branch recognition; and absence of `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_ShouldJumpIfGreaterSigned` from the C control lowering module.

The focused signed slot/slot branch contract is now guarded by same-basic-block local-written-before proof. `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_i64_written_before()` only proves an `sN` local usable when the current basic block contains an earlier write from a SemIR destination, immediate scalar constant, numeric conversion destination, or stack-copy propagation source. With that proof, the generated branch keeps frame-slot bounds and signed-type tag checks but branches directly on `if (zr_aot_sL op zr_aot_sR)` without refreshing `sN` from `zr_aot_left/right->value.nativeObject.nativeInt64` inside the branch. This deliberately does not prove cross-block joins, entry parameters, or resume/deopt restored local state.

The numeric conversion source-contract test `test_aot_c_source_lowers_typed_numeric_conversion_to_c_casts` locks the separate typed conversion lowering module, direct emitter declarations for signed/unsigned-to-float, float-to-signed/unsigned, unsigned-to-signed, and signed-to-unsigned conversion helpers, the `zr_aot_convert_signed_to_float` / `zr_aot_convert_unsigned_to_float` / `zr_aot_convert_float_to_signed` / `zr_aot_convert_unsigned_to_signed` / `zr_aot_convert_float_to_unsigned` / `zr_aot_convert_signed_to_unsigned` source markers, direct `(TZrFloat64)`, `(TZrInt64)`, and `(TZrUInt64)` cast expressions, the `zr_aot_unsigned_to_signed_limit` wrap expression, and function-body routing for `TO_FLOAT_SIGNED` / `TO_FLOAT_UNSIGNED` / `TO_INT_FLOAT` / `TO_INT_UNSIGNED` / `TO_UINT_FLOAT` / `TO_UINT_SIGNED`.

The AOT M2 typed scalar generated-product contract now also locks the first scalar C local mirror path for focused numeric conversions. `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals.c` gathers local declarations from typed local bindings, SemIR destination static C types, and focused typed numeric conversion bytecode destinations. Reused conversion temporary slots can therefore declare all proven mirrors, for example `zr_aot_s29`, `zr_aot_u29`, and `zr_aot_f29`; `backend_aot_c_scalar_conversion.c` then writes destination-local casts such as `zr_aot_f29 = (TZrFloat64)zr_aot_s2;`, `zr_aot_s29 = (TZrInt64)zr_aot_f17;`, and `zr_aot_u29 = (TZrUInt64)zr_aot_f17;` before mirroring through the existing result/frame-slot path. This is still a focused scalar subset: generic value-source conversions, non-numeric conversions, broader branch forms, and full C-local/frame-slot coherence remain later AOT plan work.

The scalar destination-local fallback mirror contract now covers arithmetic, compare, bitwise, bit-not, and shift templates whose operands are not all proven local. Those paths still validate/read frame slots into temporary result expressions, but if the destination slot has scalar-local coverage they now mirror the computed `zr_aot_s_result`, `zr_aot_u_result`, `zr_aot_f_result`, or bool compare result into `zr_aot_sN`, `zr_aot_uN`, `zr_aot_fN`, or `zr_aot_bN` before the existing frame-slot write. This keeps destination locals coherent after fallback computations without yet making locals the authoritative source for every operand.

The focused scalar stack-copy generated-product contract now keeps declared scalar source and destination locals coherent for the first bool/i64/u64/f64 copy subset. `backend_aot_c_scalar_stack_copy.c` still validates source and destination frame slots and writes the copied payload through the existing `SZrTypeValue` frame-slot ABI, but when source scalar-local coverage is proven it reads the copy payload from `zr_aot_bN`, `zr_aot_sN`, `zr_aot_uN`, or `zr_aot_fN`, and when destination scalar-local coverage is proven it mirrors the copied value into the destination local. `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals.c` also propagates scalar-local kind across `GET_STACK` / `SET_STACK` destinations when the source slot is proven local, so the focused f64 copy chain declares `zr_aot_f40`, writes `zr_aot_f40 = zr_aot_f_value`, then reads `zr_aot_f_value = zr_aot_f40` before mirroring into `zr_aot_f22`. The executable typed-scalar golden locks the bool path with `zr_aot_b_value = zr_aot_b7;` and `zr_aot_b5 = (TZrBool)(zr_aot_b_value != 0u);` before the focused `branchFlag` false branch consumes `zr_aot_b5`. This closes only the focused scalar-copy source/destination local mirror and destination-propagation slice; systematic C-local storage ownership and GC-root coherence remain later work.

The same generated-product contract now covers the first signed const branch local predicate. The focused source `if (product == 42)` quickens to `JUMP_IF_NOT_EQUAL_SIGNED_CONST`; generated C must sync the left slot into `zr_aot_s2`, emit `if (zr_aot_s2 != zr_aot_right_literal) {`, and reject the older `if (zr_aot_left_scalar != zr_aot_right_literal) {` predicate in that path. This closes only the focused signed const branch local-predicate slice, not the broader branch matrix.

The bool branch generated-product contract now also covers the focused `branchFlag` false-branch path. Generated C must keep `branchFlag` mirrored into `zr_aot_b5` during the preceding scalar stack-copy, emit the proven-local marker `zr_aot_jump_if_bool_false_scalar_local`, branch with `if (!zr_aot_b5) {`, and reject both the older `if (!zr_aot_condition_bool) {` fallback predicate and the older proven-local refresh `zr_aot_b5 = (TZrBool)(zr_aot_condition->value.nativeObject.nativeBool != 0u);`. This closes only the focused straight-line `JUMP_IF_BOOL_FALSE` condition-local predicate slice; resume/deopt entry local-state reconstruction remains later work.

The same bool branch path now uses the shared same-basic-block written-before proof instead of broad bool local declaration coverage. `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_bool_written_before()` reuses the scalar-kind proof used by signed branches and only permits `if (!zr_aot_bN)` when an earlier instruction in the current block wrote the bool local through SemIR, an immediate constant, conversion, or stack-copy propagation. The focused `branchFlag` and unsigned-compare false branches still get the no-refresh generated shape, but unproven bool branches fall back to validating the frame slot and reading `zr_aot_condition_bool`.

The focused unsigned compare branch check confirms there is no independent unsigned/f64 branch lowering entry for `if (unsignedInverted <= unsignedRight)`. That source path lowers to `zr_aot_scalar_exec_u64_compare`, writes `zr_aot_b23 = (TZrBool)(zr_aot_u21 <= zr_aot_u7);`, mirrors `zr_aot_u_result = zr_aot_b23;`, and then consumes the bool local through the existing `zr_aot_jump_if_bool_false_scalar_local` path with `if (!zr_aot_b23) {`. Broader branch coverage therefore belongs to the local-state/control-flow matrix, not to a separate unsigned branch helper.

The signed slot/slot branch generated-product contract now rejects the older `zr_aot_s2 = zr_aot_left_scalar;` and `zr_aot_s4 = zr_aot_right_scalar;` synchronization shape. Proven local operands must be copied directly from the validated frame-slot value pointers into `zr_aot_s2` and `zr_aot_s4` before the `sN` predicate. This closes only the focused fused signed slot/slot direct-sync slice.

The signed `i64` binary generated-product contract now also rejects the older `zr_aot_s0 = zr_aot_s_left;` synchronization shape on the first covered `left * right` local-expression path. Proven local operands must be copied directly from `frame.slotBase[0].value.value.nativeObject.nativeInt64` and `frame.slotBase[1].value.value.nativeObject.nativeInt64` into `zr_aot_s0` and `zr_aot_s1` before emitting `zr_aot_s2 = zr_aot_s0 * zr_aot_s1;`. This is still a focused 04-S3 frame-slot-to-`sN` sync slice rather than full C-local/frame-slot coherence.

The unsigned `u64` binary generated-product contract follows the same direct-sync rule for the first covered `unsignedLeft + unsignedRight` path. Proven local operands must be copied directly from `frame.slotBase[6].value.value.nativeObject.nativeUInt64` and `frame.slotBase[7].value.value.nativeObject.nativeUInt64` into `zr_aot_u6` and `zr_aot_u7` before emitting `zr_aot_u8 = zr_aot_u6 + zr_aot_u7;`, rejecting the older `zr_aot_u6 = zr_aot_u_left;` synchronization shape. This remains a focused scalar subset and does not yet make C locals the authoritative storage for every path.

The `f64` binary generated-product contract now follows the same direct-sync rule for the first covered `floatLeft * floatRight` path. Proven local operands must be copied directly from `frame.slotBase[17].value.value.nativeObject.nativeDouble` and `frame.slotBase[18].value.value.nativeObject.nativeDouble` into `zr_aot_f17` and `zr_aot_f18` before emitting `zr_aot_f30 = zr_aot_f17 * zr_aot_f18;`, rejecting the older `zr_aot_f17 = zr_aot_f_left;` synchronization shape. This still mirrors results back through frame slots and is not a full C-local storage model.

The signed `i64` binary bitwise generated-product contract now follows the same direct-sync rule for the first covered `masked = maskBase & left` path. Proven local operands must be copied directly from `frame.slotBase[10].value.value.nativeObject.nativeInt64` and `frame.slotBase[0].value.value.nativeObject.nativeInt64` into `zr_aot_s10` and `zr_aot_s0` before emitting `zr_aot_s14 = zr_aot_s10 & zr_aot_s0;`. The generated product rejects the older `zr_aot_s10 = zr_aot_s_left;` / `zr_aot_s0 = zr_aot_s_right;` synchronization shape for this path. Fallback bitwise lowering can still use local `zr_aot_s_left` / `zr_aot_s_right` temporaries when scalar locals are not proven; shift and bit-not direct-sync coverage remain separate slices.

The signed `i64` shift generated-product contract now follows the same direct-sync rule for the first covered `shifted = toggled << right` and `shiftedBack = shifted >> right` paths. Proven local operands must be copied directly from `frame.slotBase[13].value.value.nativeObject.nativeInt64` / `frame.slotBase[14].value.value.nativeObject.nativeInt64` and `frame.slotBase[1].value.value.nativeObject.nativeInt64` into `zr_aot_s13` / `zr_aot_s14` and `zr_aot_s1`, then check `zr_aot_s1` for the signed shift-count range before emitting `zr_aot_s17 = (TZrInt64)((TZrUInt64)zr_aot_s13 << zr_aot_s1);` or `zr_aot_s18 = zr_aot_s14 >> zr_aot_s1;`. The generated product rejects the older `zr_aot_s13 = zr_aot_s_left;`, `zr_aot_s14 = zr_aot_s_left;`, and `zr_aot_s1 = zr_aot_s_shift;` synchronization shape for these paths. Fallback shift lowering can still use local `zr_aot_s_left` / `zr_aot_s_shift` temporaries when scalar operands are not proven.

The signed `i64` bit-not generated-product contract now follows the same direct-sync rule for the first covered `inverted = ~right` path. Proven local source operands must be copied directly from `frame.slotBase[1].value.value.nativeObject.nativeInt64` into `zr_aot_s1` before emitting `zr_aot_s17 = ~zr_aot_s1;`. The generated product rejects the older `zr_aot_s1 = zr_aot_s_source;` synchronization shape for this path. Fallback bit-not lowering can still use local `zr_aot_s_source` when the source scalar local is not proven.

The unsigned `u64` binary bitwise generated-product contract now has the same direct-sync module boundary as signed `i64` bitwise. `backend_aot_write_c_scalar_u64_bitwise()` receives the current `SZrAotExecIrFunction`, checks destination/left/right with `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_has_u64_slot`, and on the proven-local path emits direct `frame.slotBase[8]` / `frame.slotBase[7]` unsigned loads into `zr_aot_u8` / `zr_aot_u7` before `zr_aot_u12 = zr_aot_u8 & zr_aot_u7;` for the focused `unsignedMasked = unsignedSum & unsignedRight` path. The fallback path can still use `zr_aot_u_left` / `zr_aot_u_right` temporaries when scalar locals are not proven. The executable typed-scalar golden now covers this path after the interpreter generic unsigned bitwise result type was fixed to preserve `ZR_VALUE_TYPE_UINT64` for unsigned operands.

The unsigned `u64` bit-not generated-product contract now follows the same boundary. `backend_aot_write_c_scalar_u64_bit_not()` receives `SZrAotExecIrFunction`, checks source/destination with `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_has_u64_slot`, and on the proven-local path emits a direct `frame.slotBase[7].value.value.nativeObject.nativeUInt64` load into `zr_aot_u7` before `zr_aot_u33 = ~zr_aot_u7;` for the focused `unsignedInverted = ~unsignedRight` path after the unsigned shift temporaries. The fallback path still uses `zr_aot_u_source` when the source local is not proven. The executable typed-scalar golden now covers this path, rejects the old `ZrCore_Stack_GetValue` / `ZR_VALUE_FAST_SET` route, and keeps the result mirrored through the existing frame slot ABI.

The unsigned `u64` shift generated-product contract now runs end to end in the focused typed-scalar executable. `compile_expression.c` preserves the original typed operands for `<<` / `>>` instead of converting the signed shift count to the unsigned result type, and selects `BITWISE_SHIFT_LEFT` / `BITWISE_SHIFT_RIGHT` when the effective typed operands include an unsigned integer. `backend_aot_write_c_scalar_u64_shift()` checks the left operand with `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_has_u64_slot`, checks the signed shift-count operand with `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_has_i64_slot`, checks the destination with `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_has_u64_slot`, and on the proven-local path emits direct `frame.slotBase` loads into `zr_aot_uN` / `zr_aot_sN`. The focused generated product now covers `unsignedShifted = unsignedSum << right` and `unsignedShiftedBack = unsignedShifted >> right`, emitting `zr_aot_scalar_exec_u64_shift`, `zr_aot_u13 = zr_aot_u8 << zr_aot_s1;`, and `zr_aot_u14 = zr_aot_u10 >> zr_aot_s1;` while keeping the forbidden `ZrCore_Stack_GetValue` / `ZR_VALUE_FAST_SET` scan at zero. Fallback shift lowering keeps `zr_aot_u_left` / `zr_aot_s_shift` temporaries for unproven operands.

The signed `i64` scalar compare generated-product contract now follows the same direct-sync rule for the first covered `product > threshold` path. Proven compare operands must be copied directly from `frame.slotBase[2].value.value.nativeObject.nativeInt64` and `frame.slotBase[4].value.value.nativeObject.nativeInt64` into `zr_aot_s2` and `zr_aot_s4` before emitting `zr_aot_b25 = (TZrBool)(zr_aot_s2 > zr_aot_s4);`. The generated product rejects the older `zr_aot_s2 = zr_aot_s_left;` / `zr_aot_s4 = zr_aot_s_right;` synchronization shape for this path. Fallback compare lowering can still use local `zr_aot_s_left` / `zr_aot_s_right` temporaries when scalar locals are not proven.

The unsigned `u64` scalar compare generated-product contract now follows the same direct-sync rule for the first covered `unsignedSum > unsignedRight` path. Proven compare operands must be copied directly from `frame.slotBase[8].value.value.nativeObject.nativeUInt64` and `frame.slotBase[7].value.value.nativeObject.nativeUInt64` into `zr_aot_u8` and `zr_aot_u7` before emitting `zr_aot_b12 = (TZrBool)(zr_aot_u8 > zr_aot_u7);`. The generated product rejects the older `zr_aot_u8 = zr_aot_u_left;` / `zr_aot_u7 = zr_aot_u_right;` synchronization shape for this path. Fallback compare lowering can still use local `zr_aot_u_left` / `zr_aot_u_right` temporaries when scalar operands are not proven.

The scalar SemIR dispatcher now keeps binary arithmetic in a separate module boundary. `backend_aot_c_scalar_semir.c` remains the small dispatcher and comparison lowering surface: it handles scalar conversion, bitwise, binary, unsigned compare, and signed compare in that order. The signed `i64`, unsigned `u64`, and `f64` binary arithmetic emitters, operand decoders, direct frame-slot-to-`sN` / `uN` / `fN` sync logic, divide/modulo guards, and plain scalar result writers live in `backend_aot_c_scalar_binary.{h,c}`. The source-contract test reads both the dispatcher and binary module, so future binary arithmetic changes should land in the binary module instead of growing the dispatcher again.

`backend_aot_c_value_semir.c` is verified with constrained GCC/Clang syntax checks because the archived AOT backend is not in the active CMake target graph. The focused AOT C syntax checks now cover the frame cleanup, function body, value SemIR, control lowering, values lowering, legacy int arithmetic, typed arithmetic, load-const arithmetic, load-stack arithmetic, and backend gating sources with the public include paths and public `SZrAotWriterOptions` declaration, so the source-contract test is backed by direct compiler coverage for the touched AOT C emitters.

The test first failed on the missing typed arithmetic lowering contract, then passed after `backend_aot_c_lowering_typed_arithmetic.c` was added and the function-body dispatcher was updated. Dynamic member/index value access now has an explicit generated-C boundary. `GET_MEMBER`, `GET_MEMBER_SLOT`, `GET_BY_INDEX`, `SET_MEMBER`, `SET_MEMBER_SLOT`, and `SET_BY_INDEX` emit `zr_aot_value_unsupported_dynamic_value_access` after any proven value SemIR member-slot direct lowering attempt, record opcode/operand slots/member-cache-index metadata, report `unsupported AOT dynamic value access`, and fail through `ZR_AOT_C_FAIL()` instead of calling the old AOT runtime instruction helpers. This keeps dynamic object/array/string/member semantics out of direct C lowering until a static metadata contract exists.

The generated get-global fixture contains `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_GetGlobal(state, &frame, 0)` and rejects the old generated direct global value-copy template.

Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 typed bool logical scalar-local validation removes another register/SZrValue double-write case from the bool path. `backend_aot_write_c_direct_logical_equal_bool()`, `backend_aot_write_c_direct_logical_not_equal_bool()`, and `backend_aot_write_c_direct_logical_not_bool()` now receive the instruction index, consult bool scalar-local write history, and emit direct `zr_aot_bN` assignments for proven bool-local sources and destinations. Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 bool binary logical opcode scalar-local validation applies the same local-only rule to `LOGICAL_AND` and `LOGICAL_OR` bytecode lowering. `backend_aot_write_c_direct_logical_and()` and `backend_aot_write_c_direct_logical_or()` now receive the instruction index, use bool result-skip and left/right written-before proofs, and emit `zr_aot_bool_binary_scalar_local` with a direct `zr_aot_bN` assignment when the proof holds. Scalar-local write/consumer analysis now recognizes `LOGICAL_AND` / `LOGICAL_OR` bool inputs and declared bool destinations. The source-level `&&` / `||` compiler path still usually emits short-circuit branches before these opcodes, so validation for this slice is a source-contract/static generator-shape check plus the existing logical and aggregate shared-library smoke regressions.

Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 string equality bool-result scalar-local validation removes the destination value-slot write from proven string equality bool results. `backend_aot_write_c_direct_logical_equal_string()` and `backend_aot_write_c_direct_logical_not_equal_string()` now receive the instruction index and can emit `zr_aot_string_logical_bool_scalar_local` when the bool destination can skip its value slot. Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 typed power scalar-local validation removes destination value-slot writes from proven typed power results. `backend_aot_write_c_direct_pow_signed()`, `backend_aot_write_c_direct_pow_unsigned()`, and `backend_aot_write_c_direct_pow_float()` now receive the function IR and instruction index, consult result-skip and operand written-before proofs, and emit `zr_aot_arith_exec_*_power_scalar_local` direct assignments to `zr_aot_sN`, `zr_aot_uN`, or `zr_aot_fN` when safe. Unproven paths keep the old frame/value fallback. A regression check found that declaring every primitive `GET_CONSTANT` destination as a scalar local could skip value-slot writes still needed by call/shared-library runtime boundaries, so scalar-local analysis now declares immediate constants only when they feed typed power operands. Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 static direct-call u64/f64 scalar-local sync validation extends the existing static direct-call local restoration boundary beyond i64/bool. `backend_aot_write_c_static_direct_function_call()` now emits `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_SyncUnsignedIntLocal()` and `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_SyncFloatLocal()` guarded by u64/f64 local-slot checks, while continuing to reject generated `zr_aot_direct_call_result` payload reads. Scalar-local analysis records non-tail call opcodes as result writes and back-propagates a stack-copy destination kind only when the source slot is a call-result destination; this targeted rule fixes no-arg `uint`/`float` static callees copied into typed locals without reintroducing the broad copy propagation that incorrectly scalarized inline-struct value-type slots. Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 MethodInfo signature descriptor validation replaces the old null signature placeholder with a generated per-function descriptor. The public AOT ABI now defines `SZrAotSignatureType` and `SZrAotSignature`; `backend_aot_c_emitter.c` emits `zr_aot_signature_N_types` and `zr_aot_signature_N` from each function's typed return/parameter metadata and stores `&zr_aot_signature_N` in `SZrAotMethodInfo.signature`. The value typed-call shared-library smoke locks the generated shape for a one-parameter callee, including `parameterCount`, non-null `returnType`, and non-null `parameterTypes`. This is the signature metadata source required by later typed-to-typed native C signature routing; it does not yet replace current helper-based static direct calls or inline-struct call/return boundaries with direct typed C call/return lowering. Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 MethodInfo table publication validation makes the generated signature descriptors reachable from the public compiled-module descriptor. The AOT ABI is now version 3 and `ZrAotCompiledModule` exposes `methodInfos` plus `methodInfoCount`; `backend_aot_c_emitter.c` emits a `zr_aot_method_infos[]` table that points at every generated `zr_aot_method_info_N`, then publishes that table and the function count in `zr_aot_compiled_module`. The shared-library smoke loads the generated module and verifies that `module->methodInfos[0]->signature` is non-null. This still remains metadata publication only: typed-to-typed direct C call/return lowering, `in` / `out` writeback, and deopt/dynamic bridge boxing templates remain separate 07-S5 follow-up work. Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 static no-arg i64 typed thunk direct-call validation adds the first typed-to-typed direct C call slice. The C emitter recognizes typed no-argument functions with int64 return metadata whose body is a constant signed-int return and emits `zr_aot_typed_i64_fn_N` forward declarations and definitions returning `TZrInt64`. Function-body call lowering routes eligible static no-arg i64 call destinations directly through that thunk, assigns the scalar local, and then syncs the destination stack slot with `ZR_VALUE_FAST_SET` so still-frame-backed later consumers remain correct until the wider 07 cleanup removes them. The dedicated shared-library smoke executes `answer(): int { return 42; }` through the direct path, verifies the typed thunk markers, and rejects generated `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_CallStaticDirect` / `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_CallStackValue` in that path. This is intentionally narrow: typed parameter ABI, general returns, inline structs, `in` / `out` writeback, and deopt/dynamic bridge boxing remain follow-up 07-S5 work. WSL GCC validation reports call contracts 5/0, typed direct-call shared-library smoke 1/0, and aggregate shared-library smoke 8/0.

Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 static one-arg i64 typed thunk direct-call validation extends the typed-to-typed path with the first direct C parameter ABI slice. The C emitter recognizes single-parameter typed i64 functions whose body returns parameter slot 0 and emits `zr_aot_typed_i64_fn_N(struct SZrState *state, TZrInt64 zr_aot_arg0)`, returning the C argument directly. Function-body call lowering proves the call window's first argument slot (`functionSlot + 1`) is an initialized i64 scalar local before the call and emits `zr_aot_typed_i64_fn_N(state, zr_aot_sArg)` instead of `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_CallStaticDirect`. The destination still syncs its stack slot with `ZR_VALUE_FAST_SET` for current frame-backed consumers. The dedicated shared-library smoke now executes `echo(value: int): int { return value; }` through this route and rejects generated `CallStaticDirect` / `CallStackValue` for the direct typed path. This remains a narrow one-arg identity-return foothold; multi-arg calls, non-identity/general typed returns, inline structs, `in` / `out` writeback, deopt/dynamic bridge boxing, and stack-sync removal remain later 07-S5 work. WSL GCC validation reports call contracts 5/0, typed direct-call shared-library smoke 2/0, and the broader focused AOT group passing call, shared-library, value-type, power, source, generic numeric, global, logical, typed-scalar, return, and frame-setup binaries.

Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 static i64 typed direct-call stack-sync elision validation removes that temporary destination stack-slot sync for the existing no-arg and one-arg direct-thunk routes when scalar-local liveness proves it is unnecessary. The typed direct-call writers now receive `syncStackSlot`; function-body routing computes it from `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_i64_result_can_skip_value_slot(functionIr, destinationSlot, instructionIndex)`. When later reachable consumers can read `zr_aot_sN`, generated C keeps only the direct C call assignment and omits `SZrTypeValue *zr_aot_typed_destination`, `zr_aot_static_i64_*_direct_call_sync_stack_slot`, and typed-destination `ZR_VALUE_FAST_SET`. The fallback path still writes the stack slot for frame-backed consumers, so this is not a global removal. Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 static one-arg i64 arg+constant typed thunk validation broadens the first direct C parameter ABI foothold from identity returns to `return arg0 + signed-constant`. The emitter recognizes both older bytecode add-constant shapes and the SemIR scalar binary form generated as `ADD_SIGNED_LOAD_STACK_CONST` followed by `FUNCTION_RETURN`, then emits `zr_aot_typed_i64_fn_N(struct SZrState *state, TZrInt64 zr_aot_arg0)` with a direct `(TZrInt64)(zr_aot_arg0 + (TZrInt64)K)` return. The dedicated shared-library smoke executes `inc(value: int): int { return value + 1; }` through the one-arg typed direct-call path, verifies runtime result `42`, rejects `CallStaticDirect` / `CallStackValue`, and keeps the scalar-only destination free of typed-destination stack sync. Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 static two-arg i64 typed thunk validation adds the next narrow typed parameter ABI slice. The emitter recognizes typed two-parameter i64 functions whose body returns `arg0 + arg1`, including `ADD_SIGNED`, `ADD_SIGNED_PLAIN_DEST`, and the current SemIR scalar binary `ADD_SIGNED_LOAD_STACK` form followed by `FUNCTION_RETURN`, then emits `zr_aot_typed_i64_fn_N(struct SZrState *state, TZrInt64 zr_aot_arg0, TZrInt64 zr_aot_arg1)` with a direct `(TZrInt64)(zr_aot_arg0 + zr_aot_arg1)` return. Function-body call lowering proves both call-window arguments, `functionSlot + 1` and `functionSlot + 2`, are initialized i64 scalar locals before emitting `zr_aot_static_i64_two_arg_direct_call`; scalar-only destinations continue to omit the typed-destination stack sync. The dedicated shared-library smoke executes `sum(left: int, right: int): int { return left + right; }`, verifies runtime result `42`, rejects `CallStaticDirect` / `CallStackValue`, and raises the typed direct-call smoke count to 4/0. Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 static two-arg i64 subtract typed thunk validation broadens that same two-parameter route from addition to `return arg0 - arg1`. The emitter recognizes `SUB_SIGNED` and `SUB_SIGNED_PLAIN_DEST` followed by `FUNCTION_RETURN`, then emits the same two-argument C thunk signature returning `(TZrInt64)(zr_aot_arg0 - zr_aot_arg1)`. The call-routing proof and direct-call writer are unchanged from the two-arg add slice, so eligible static calls continue to pass both i64 scalar locals directly and skip typed-destination stack sync when the destination stays scalar-local-only. The dedicated shared-library smoke executes `diff(left: int, right: int): int { return left - right; }`, verifies runtime result `42`, rejects `CallStaticDirect` / `CallStackValue`, and raises the typed direct-call smoke count to 5/0. Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 static two-arg i64 multiply typed thunk validation extends that same two-parameter route to `return arg0 * arg1`. The emitter recognizes `MUL_SIGNED`, `MUL_SIGNED_PLAIN_DEST`, and the SemIR scalar binary `MUL_SIGNED_LOAD_STACK` form followed by `FUNCTION_RETURN`, then emits the same two-argument C thunk signature returning `(TZrInt64)(zr_aot_arg0 * zr_aot_arg1)`. The existing call-routing proof and direct-call writer are reused, so eligible static calls pass both initialized i64 scalar locals directly and keep scalar-only destinations free of typed-destination stack sync. A new focused arithmetic shared-library smoke target executes `product(left: int, right: int): int { return left * right; }`, verifies runtime result `42`, rejects `CallStaticDirect` / `CallStackValue`, and keeps additional arithmetic coverage out of the already large typed direct-call smoke file. Focused 2026-06-23 07-S5 no-arg local-constant typed direct-call validation tightens the i64/bool/u64/f64 no-argument cases from runtime static-call fallback to typed-to-typed direct C calls. `backend_aot_c_try_get_i64_constant_return()`, `backend_aot_c_try_get_bool_constant_return()`, and `backend_aot_c_try_get_f64_constant_return()` now accept the compiler shape `GET_CONSTANT -> GET_STACK/SET_STACK copy -> FUNCTION_RETURN`; `backend_aot_c_try_get_u64_constant_return()` accepts the same local-copy shape and the current unsigned conversion shape with `TO_UINT` or `TO_UINT_SIGNED` before `FUNCTION_RETURN`. Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 static one-arg f64 divide-constant typed thunk validation broadens the one-parameter floating-point direct-call route to ordered `return arg0 / nonzero-float-constant`. `backend_aot_c_typed_f64_thunks.c` now recognizes float/double callable returns with one float/double parameter, no varargs, an optional parameter-copy prefix, `GET_CONSTANT`, `DIV_FLOAT`, and `FUNCTION_RETURN` of the divide result. The recognizer deliberately requires the argument on the left and the constant on the right, then rejects `0.0` constants before allowing the direct route; dynamic denominators and zero-denominator failure behavior remain outside this direct thunk. The emitted thunk keeps the one-argument ABI `static TZrFloat64 zr_aot_typed_f64_fn_N(struct SZrState *state, TZrFloat64 zr_aot_arg0)` and directly returns `(TZrFloat64)(zr_aot_arg0 / (TZrFloat64)K)`. The existing f64 one-arg direct-call writer and route proof are reused, so generated C assigns `zr_aot_fD = zr_aot_typed_f64_fn_N(state, zr_aot_fA)` and omits destination stack sync when scalar-local consumers can use the C local. The f64 smoke now executes `halve(value)` with `84.0 / 2.0`, verifies runtime result 42, and rejects `CallStaticDirect`, `CallStackValue`, and unnecessary typed-destination sync. Focused 2026-06-04 typed numeric conversion validation added `tests/parser/test_typed_numeric_conversion.c` and registered `zr_vm_typed_numeric_conversion_test`. The signed-to-float case compiles `return <float> i` for a statically `int` source, verifies `TO_FLOAT_SIGNED` is emitted without generic `TO_FLOAT`, executes through generated-frame slots, and returns float `7.0`. The unsigned-to-float case compiles `return <float> u` for a statically `uint` source, verifies `TO_FLOAT_UNSIGNED` is emitted without generic `TO_FLOAT`, executes through generated-frame slots, and returns float `9.0`. The float-to-signed case compiles `return <int> f` for a statically `float` source, verifies `TO_INT_FLOAT` is emitted without generic `TO_INT`, executes through generated-frame slots, and returns integer `2`. The unsigned-to-signed case compiles `return <int> u` for a statically `uint` source, verifies `TO_INT_UNSIGNED` is emitted without generic `TO_INT`, executes through generated-frame slots, and returns integer `17`; a high-bit boundary case materializes `<uint>-1`, converts it back through `TO_INT_UNSIGNED`, and returns `-1` with C# unchecked-style wrap semantics. The float-to-unsigned case compiles `return <uint> f` for a statically `float` source, verifies `TO_UINT_FLOAT` is emitted without generic `TO_UINT`, executes through generated-frame slots, and returns unsigned integer `12`. The signed-to-unsigned case compiles `return <uint> i` for a statically negative `int` source, verifies `TO_UINT_SIGNED` is emitted without generic `TO_UINT`, executes through generated-frame slots, and returns the modulo unsigned payload. The AOT C source contract now also requires `backend_aot_c_lowering_typed_conversion.c`, direct function-body routing, explicit C cast expressions, and the deterministic unsigned-to-signed wrap formula for those six proven numeric conversion forms.

Focused 2026-06-03 validation for the POD return, typed call/return SemIR, first M5 AOT expression-contract slice, executable inline-copy lowering, primitive field load/store lowering, and first typed call/return executable lowering slice passed on WSL GCC and WSL Clang for `zr_vm_semir_pipeline_test`, `zr_vm_instruction_execution_test`, `zr_vm_compiler_integration_test`, and `zr_vm_value_type_runtime_test`. Focused 2026-06-24 08-S1 generic instantiation table validation starts the generic sharing phase without touching AOT code generation yet. `zr_vm_parser/include/zr_vm_parser/generic_instantiation.h` and `zr_vm_parser/src/zr_vm_parser/generic_instantiation.c` now define `SZrGenericInstantiationTable` and `SZrGenericInstantiationRecord`, recording `baseToken`, concrete type arguments, resolved reference/value shape, `shareKind`, and stable `cInstanceId`. The table deduplicates by base token plus argument signature and classifies instances with il2cpp-style sharing rules: all reference-shaped arguments share, while any value-shaped argument monomorphizes. The default entry point infers shape from `EZrValueType`, and the resolved entry point lets the compiler later pass source class/struct shape explicitly so inline structs are not accidentally shared. RED was the new `zr_vm_generic_instantiation_test` target failing to compile because `zr_vm_parser/generic_instantiation.h` did not exist. GREEN passed `zr_vm_generic_instantiation_test` 3/0, CTest `generic_instantiation` 1/1, and related `zr_vm_type_inference_test` 118/0. This closes only 08-S1; 08-S2 constraints, 08-S3 monomorphized C generation, 08-S4 generic dictionary, 08-S5 generic `CALL_TYPED`, 08-S6 dynamic-instance deopt, and 08-S7 full-AOT enforcement remain open.

Focused 2026-06-24 08-S2 generic constraint validation closes the planned compile-time constraint check acceptance without changing production inference logic. Existing type inference already covered named constraints, source interface implementation, class/struct constraints, owner constraints, exact unique/shared/weak ownership constraints, and native generic constraint mismatches. The missing independent `new()` coverage now lives in `tests/parser/test_generic_constraints.c`: `NeedNew<DefaultCtor>` succeeds while `NeedNew<AbstractThing>` fails with `new() constraint`. The first build attempt proved the new target was not registered in the current CMake tree; after reconfiguration, `zr_vm_generic_constraints_test` passed 1/0, CTest `generic_constraints` passed 1/1, parser tests passed 75/0, and type inference passed 118/0. This closes only 08-S2; 08-S3 monomorphized C generation, 08-S4 generic dictionary, 08-S5 generic `CALL_TYPED`, 08-S6 dynamic-instance deopt, and 08-S7 full-AOT enforcement remain open.

Focused 2026-06-24 08-S3 generic monomorphization validation adds the first closed value-generic AOT generation slice. `backend_aot_c_generic_monomorphization.{h,c}` scans closed generic inline struct frame slots and emits a `zr_aot_generic_monomorphization_table` marker, fallback `ZrLayout_<id>` inline layout declaration, and `zr_fn_pair__*` monomorphized wrapper for `Pair<int,int>`. `type_inference_core.c` finalizes closed generic instance field layouts from concrete primitive arguments, `compiler_typed_metadata.c` now prefers exact closed layout names before open generic fallback, and `function_type_layout.c` can conservatively resolve an open generic layout id to the unique closed instance layout in the same prototype table. The runtime constructor receiver copy-back in `function.c` now accepts compatible resolved inline layouts even when open and closed layout ids differ. RED first found missing monomorphization markers/layouts, then inline typed-call failure, `COPY_STACK` missing inline layout, and finally runtime result 0; GREEN passes the generated shared-library `Pair<int,int>` case with result 81.
