This closes only 08-S3; shared-reference generic dictionaries, generic `CALL_TYPED`, dynamic-instance deopt, and full-AOT missing-instance enforcement remain open.

Focused 2026-06-24 08-S4 generic reference sharing adds the first dictionary-backed shared-reference AOT shape. The public AOT ABI is now version 4 and defines `EZrAotGenericSlotKind`, `SZrAotGenericSlot`, `SZrAotGenericResolvedSlot`, and `SZrAotGenericDictionary`; `SZrAotMethodInfo` carries a `genericDictionary` pointer so dictionary state stays at the function boundary instead of becoming statement-flow state. `aot_runtime_generic_dictionary.c` implements lazy TYPE_LAYOUT and SIZEOF slot resolution with per-dictionary cache storage. `backend_aot_c_generic_sharing.{h,c}` scans reference-like closed generic typed locals, emits one dictionary per concrete reference instance, emits one `zr_fn_<base>__shared` function per generic base, and publishes `ZrAot_GenericSlot_*` generated C access macros. The 08-S4 acceptance test proves `Box<RefA>` and `Box<RefB>` produce two dictionaries but one shared `zr_fn_box__shared`, verifies MethodInfo dictionary attachment, compiles the generated C shared library, and directly validates lazy slot cache behavior. WSL GCC validation passes `zr_vm_aot_c_generic_reference_sharing_test` 2/0, CTest `aot_c_generic_reference_sharing` 1/1, frame setup contracts 1/0, source contracts 19/0, method-info signature 1/0, and generic monomorphization 1/0. Generic `CALL_TYPED` dispatch through dictionary METHOD slots remains the 08-S5 boundary; dynamic-instance deopt and full-AOT missing-instance diagnostics remain open.

Focused 2026-06-24 08-S5A generic CALL_TYPED METHOD-slot carrier validation adds the dictionary method-entry half of the planned dual-shape generic call lowering. `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_GenericSlot_Method()` now lazily resolves and caches `ZR_AOT_GENERIC_SLOT_METHOD` as an `FZrAotEntryThunk`; generated C publishes `ZrAot_GenericSlot_Method(dict, slot)`, emits a METHOD slot per shared reference generic dictionary, and has `zr_fn_<base>__shared` retrieve and call the method thunk from the dictionary. The monomorphized wrapper path now carries a `zr_aot_generic_call_typed_monomorphized_direct` marker around its direct concrete specialization call. RED was the new `zr_vm_aot_c_generic_call_typed_test` failing to link because the METHOD-slot runtime helper did not exist; GREEN passes the new test 2/0, reference sharing 2/0, monomorphization 1/0, source contracts 19/0, frame setup contracts 1/0, method-info signature 1/0, and CTest `aot_c_generic_monomorphization` / `aot_c_generic_reference_sharing` / `aot_c_generic_call_typed` 3/3. This is deliberately recorded as 08-S5A only: source-level generic `CALL_TYPED` route selection and AOT/interpreter result equality remain open for 08-S5B.

Focused 2026-06-24 08-S5 generic CALL_TYPED validation closes the planned monomorphized/shared generic call lowering slice. The value SemIR `CALL_TYPED` writer now receives callee typed metadata and can recognize a source-level reference generic callee such as `func stamp<T>(value: T): Stamp where T: class`; for that shared-reference route it emits a callsite-local `ZR_AOT_GENERIC_SLOT_METHOD` dictionary, resolves the method through `ZrAot_GenericSlot_Method()`, and passes the resulting `zr_aot_fn_*` thunk into `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_CallInlineStruct()`. Non-shared/monomorphized paths keep the direct concrete `zr_aot_fn_*` call shape and the earlier `zr_aot_generic_call_typed_monomorphized_direct` marker. Typed metadata construction now recognizes current function/method generic parameters and temporarily sets the current declaration while building script typed export metadata, so generic parameter `T` survives into callee parameter metadata for AOT route proof. RED was the remaining 08-S5A gap: generated METHOD-slot carriers existed, but source-level generic `CALL_TYPED` did not choose the shared METHOD-slot callsite and had no AOT/interpreter equality test. GREEN passes `zr_vm_aot_c_generic_call_typed_test` 3/0; the new reference generic call test compiles a project binary, generates and builds the AOT C shared library, executes via `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_ExecuteEntry`, and returns the same `42` as the interpreter. Related validation passes reference sharing 2/0, monomorphization 1/0, source contracts 19/0, frame setup contracts 1/0, method-info signature 1/0, type inference, and CTest generic AOT selection 3/3. This closes 08-S5 only; 08-S6 dynamic-instance deopt and 08-S7 full-AOT missing-instance diagnostics remain open.

Focused 2026-06-24 08-S6A generic CALL_TYPED missing-instance deopt validation adds the first executable fallback for a shared-reference generic method slot that cannot resolve to an AOT entry. `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_CallInlineStructDynamicDeoptBridge()` now validates the generated deopt id, prepares the call window for an inline-struct-return VM call, copies value arguments from the AOT frame, invokes the callable through the interpreter with the inline destination as return destination, and restores the AOT frame. Generated shared generic `CALL_TYPED` code now keeps the fast `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_CallInlineStruct()` route when `ZrAot_GenericSlot_Method()` returns a thunk, but emits `zr_aot_generic_call_typed_missing_instance_deopt` and calls the new bridge when the METHOD slot is missing. RED was the 08-S5 shape where a missing METHOD slot called `ZR_AOT_C_FAIL()`; GREEN passes `zr_vm_aot_c_generic_call_typed_test` 5/0, including a test that rewrites the generated METHOD slot to `.staticMethod = ZR_NULL`, rebuilds the generated shared library, executes through AOT, and gets the same `42` as the interpreter via fallback. The existing dynamic deopt bridge smoke remains green at 2/0. This is only 08-S6A: it proves the missing AOT method entry fallback path, but reflective `MakeGenericType` / runtime dynamic generic instance construction is still open for full 08-S6, and full-AOT diagnostics remain 08-S7.

Focused 2026-06-24 08-S7A full-AOT generic CALL_TYPED no-deopt validation adds the first visible full-AOT switch in the AOT C writer without claiming the later reachability/manifest closure work. `SZrAotWriterOptions` now exposes `requireFullAot`, and the C emitter passes it through function-body generation into value SemIR `CALL_TYPED` lowering. Default hybrid mode is unchanged: shared generic METHOD-slot calls still emit `zr_aot_generic_call_typed_missing_instance_deopt` and `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_CallInlineStructDynamicDeoptBridge()` when a METHOD slot is missing. With `requireFullAot = ZR_TRUE`, the same source-level reference generic call emits `zr_aot_generic_call_typed_full_aot_no_deopt`, keeps the static `ZrAot_GenericSlot_Method()` plus `CallInlineStruct()` fast path, and directly fails if the METHOD slot is null instead of deopting to the interpreter. RED was the absence of any full-AOT writer option and generated deopt suppression; GREEN passes `zr_vm_aot_c_generic_call_typed_test` 6/0, including a full-AOT generated shared-library run that returns the same `42` as the interpreter while the generated C contains no missing-instance deopt marker, no dynamic deopt bridge call, and no `"generic call typed missing AOT instance"` label. This is only 08-S7A: compile-time diagnostics for uncollected generic instances still require the 12-S8 reachability/manifest/full-AOT closure graph and the broader 10/12 reflection-preservation machinery.

Focused 2026-06-24 09-S1A GC descriptor offset-list validation adds the first AOT memory-management descriptor slice. `ZrCore_TypeLayout_VisitGcValues()` now uses `layout->gcFieldOffsets` directly for non-union struct layouts when metadata offsets are present, so the GC visitor can follow the same offset-list descriptor the AOT path emits instead of re-deriving locations from the field table. The AOT C type-layout emitter now generates `ZrGcOffsets_<id>[]` plus `ZrGcDescriptor_<id>` for inline struct layouts with `gcFieldCount > 0`, validates each offset against the struct byte size and `SZrTypeValue` width, and emits no descriptor for blittable/POD layouts with no GC fields. RED was the generated C surface only containing `ZrLayout_*` plus static size/align/offset asserts, and the core scan path ignoring metadata offset tables. GREEN passes `zr_vm_value_type_runtime_test` 14/0, including a metadata-offset test where the field table is deliberately not the source of truth, `zr_vm_aot_c_value_type_shared_library_smoke_test` 2/0, including generated-C checks that string-field structs emit a descriptor while int-only structs do not, and `zr_vm_aot_c_type_layout_contracts_test` 1/0. This is only 09-S1A: the generated descriptor is now present as a static AOT C carrier, but full 09-S1 still needs the AOT MethodInfo/module metadata registration path so runtime-loaded AOT layouts consume the generated descriptor directly.

Focused 2026-06-24 10-S1A reflection metadata-level validation adds the first concrete reflection-tier carrier to the AOT ABI without claiming the later trim/reachability behavior. `ZR_VM_AOT_ABI_VERSION` is now 5, `EZrAotReflectionMetadataLevel` defines `NONE`, `RUNTIME_MAPPING`, and `DESCRIPTION`, and `SZrAotMethodInfo` carries `reflectionMetadataLevel` plus reserved bytes for future ABI expansion. Generated MethodInfo records now default to `ZR_AOT_REFLECTION_METADATA_RUNTIME_MAPPING`, making dynamic call/token mapping an explicit per-method runtime contract while leaving full descriptive metadata for later annotation/manifest retention work. RED was the absence of any MethodInfo reflection-tier field and a stale hard-coded ABI mismatch expectation; GREEN passes `zr_vm_aot_c_frame_setup_contracts_test` 1/0, `zr_vm_aot_c_shared_library_smoke_test` 8/0 with a runtime descriptor assertion for `RUNTIME_MAPPING`, and `zr_vm_aot_c_descriptor_diagnostics_test` 1/0 with ABI diagnostics tied to the current header constant. This is only 10-S1A: type/member-level default-minimal metadata, size reduction measurement, and `DESCRIPTION` preservation still require the 10/12 reachability and retention pipeline.

Focused 2026-06-24 11-S1A zrp metadata header validation adds the first concrete data-metadata container surface for the two-segment zrp plan. `zr_vm_core/zrp_metadata.h` now defines a fixed 80-byte little-endian `SZrZrpMetadataHeader` with four `SZrZrpMetadataSection` directory entries: token records, string pool, signature blob pool, and constant pool. `zrp_metadata.c` provides init, validate, write, and read helpers that can round-trip the header and reject invalid mmap-style views such as bad magic, future versions, wrong header size, section data before the header, and counted sections without an element size. RED was the new zrp metadata format target failing after reconfiguration because `zr_vm_core/zrp_metadata.h` did not exist; GREEN passes `zr_vm_zrp_metadata_format_test` 2/0, `zr_vm_metadata_runtime_query_test` 3/0, `zr_vm_metadata_token_model_test` 21/0, and CTest `zrp_metadata_format|metadata_runtime_query|metadata_token_model` 3/3. This is only 11-S1A: actual TypeDef/MethodDef/FieldDef table export, string/signature pool materialization, zrp manifest file IO, code registration, and lazy token resolution remain open.

Focused 2026-06-24 11-S1B zrp definition-table directory validation expands that data-metadata container to the first ECMA-style definition-table ABI. `ZR_ZRP_METADATA_VERSION` is now 2, the fixed header is 208 bytes, and `SZrZrpMetadataHeader` carries 12 ordered section directories: token records; TypeDef, MethodDef, FieldDef, GenericParam, GenericParamConstraint, TypeSpec, MethodSpec, ModuleRef; and the string/signature/constant pools. `zrp_metadata.h` defines compact row carriers for those definition tables, and `zrp_metadata.c` now validates counted sections against the expected row width or byte-pool width instead of accepting any nonzero element size. RED was the zrp metadata format test failing to compile when it required the new section kinds, header fields, and row types. GREEN passes `zr_vm_zrp_metadata_format_test` 3/0, including full 12-section round-trip and rejection of malformed definition-table element sizes. This is still 11-S1: it establishes the table directory and row ABI, but compiler export of actual rows, pool materialization, zrp manifest file IO, code registration, and lazy token resolution remain open.

Focused 2026-06-24 11-S1C zrp mmap section-view validation adds the first read-only payload access API on top of the version-2 directory. `SZrZrpMetadataSectionView` and `ZrCore_ZrpMetadata_GetSectionView()` let callers resolve a section kind to the validated directory entry, payload pointer, byte length, count, and element size from an mmap-style buffer. The helper revalidates the header before exposing pointers, treats empty sections as valid empty views, and clears the output view on truncated buffers or unknown section kinds. RED was the format test failing to compile when it required the new view type/API. GREEN passes `zr_vm_zrp_metadata_format_test` 4/0, including TypeDef and string-pool payload resolution plus empty constant-pool and invalid-view rejection. This is still only the section payload access layer; high-level token/type/method/field resolution remains later 11-S3/11-S4 work.

Focused 2026-06-24 11-S1D zrp definition-table token validation adds the first row-level semantic guardrail to the zrp data-metadata format. `ZrCore_ZrpMetadata_ValidateDefinitionTables()` walks the version-2 section views and checks that each definition row carries the expected metadata token table tag: TypeDef rows require TYPE_DEF tokens; MethodDef and FieldDef rows require MEMBER_DEF tokens owned by TYPE_DEF; generic params are owned by TYPE_DEF or MEMBER_DEF; generic constraints point to type tokens; TypeSpec rows require TYPE_SPEC tokens; MethodSpec rows use SIGNATURE tokens and point at member def/ref tokens; ModuleRef rows require ASSEMBLY_REF tokens. RED was the format test linking against a missing validation API. GREEN passes `zr_vm_zrp_metadata_format_test` 5/0, including rejection of wrong TypeDef token tags, wrong MethodDef owner tags, and wrong MethodSpec method-token tags. This is still format validation, not cross-table RID resolution or runtime metadata cache lookup.

Focused 2026-06-24 11-S1E zrp definition-table range validation tightens the same format guardrail with basic RID and child-range checks. `ZrCore_ZrpMetadata_ValidateDefinitionTables()` now rejects MethodDef and FieldDef owners whose TYPE_DEF RID is outside the TypeDef table, rejects GenericParam owner/constraint indexes that do not exist, and rejects TypeDef method/field/generic-param ranges that run past the corresponding section count. RED was a new cross-table range test failing at runtime because those invalid rows still passed validation. GREEN passes `zr_vm_zrp_metadata_format_test` 6/0. This still does not build a full resolver or cross-module symbol/token binding; it prevents malformed zrp payloads from entering later lazy metadata parsing.

Focused 2026-06-24 11-S1F zrp pool slice validation adds the bounded byte-pool read primitive needed before strings, signature blobs, and constants can be materialized safely. `SZrZrpMetadataPoolSliceView` and `ZrCore_ZrpMetadata_GetPoolSlice()` resolve offset/length pairs only inside the three byte-pool sections: string pool, signature blob pool, and constant pool. The API permits zero-length slices at the pool end, rejects non-pool section kinds and out-of-range slices, and clears the output slice on failure. RED was the format test failing to compile when it required the pool slice type/API. GREEN passes `zr_vm_zrp_metadata_format_test` 7/0, including all three pools, a pool-end empty slice, non-pool rejection, and bounds rejection. Actual pool content generation and signature/string decoding remain open.

Focused 2026-06-24 11-S1G zrp pool payload writer adds the matching write primitive for the same three byte-pool sections. `ZrCore_ZrpMetadata_WritePoolPayload()` writes a complete string/signature/constant pool payload into an already validated zrp metadata buffer, rejects non-pool section kinds, non-empty null payloads, payload length mismatches, and truncated buffers, and allows a 0-length empty pool write as a no-op with `ZR_NULL`. RED was the zrp metadata format test linking against the missing writer API. GREEN passes WSL gcc and WSL clang `zr_vm_zrp_metadata_format_test` 8/0 plus filtered metadata CTest 3/3 on both toolchains; the Windows MSVC CLI smoke still prints `hello world`. This closes byte-pool payload write plumbing only; definition-table export, string decoding, signature blob parsing, file-level zrp manifest read/write, and dump/diff tooling remain open.

Focused 2026-06-24 11-S1H zrp definition table payload writer adds the row-array write primitive for TypeDef, MethodDef, FieldDef, GenericParam, GenericParamConstraint, TypeSpec, MethodSpec, and ModuleRef sections. `ZrCore_ZrpMetadata_WriteDefinitionTablePayload()` writes a complete definition-table payload only when the caller-provided row count and element size match the section directory, and rejects pool sections, non-empty null row payloads, mismatched count or row width, and truncated buffers. RED was the zrp metadata format test linking against the missing table writer API. GREEN passes WSL gcc and WSL clang `zr_vm_zrp_metadata_format_test` 9/0 plus filtered metadata CTest 3/3 on both toolchains; the Windows MSVC CLI smoke still prints `hello world`. This closes format-layer table payload writes only; compiler export from real symbol/type/function metadata, string decoding, signature blob parsing, file-level zrp manifest read/write, and dump/diff tooling remain open.

Focused 2026-06-24 11-S1I zrp string pool view decoder adds the first semantic reader on top of the bounded string pool bytes. `SZrZrpMetadataStringView` and `ZrCore_ZrpMetadata_GetString()` resolve a string-pool offset to a NUL-terminated view and return the byte length without the terminator. The reader rejects offsets at or beyond the pool length and strings whose terminator is missing before the pool end, clearing the output on failure. RED was the zrp metadata format test failing to compile because the string view type/API did not exist. GREEN passes WSL gcc and WSL clang `zr_vm_zrp_metadata_format_test` 10/0 plus filtered metadata CTest 3/3 on both toolchains; the Windows MSVC CLI smoke still prints `hello world`. This is only string-pool view decoding; UTF-8 validation, compiler string-pool export, signature blob parsing, file-level zrp manifest read/write, and dump/diff tooling remain open.

Focused 2026-06-24 11-S1J zrp signature blob structural validator adds the first bounded parser for standalone signature blobs. `ZrCore_ZrpMetadata_ValidateSignatureBlob()` walks method signatures, field signatures, generic instance type signatures, primitive/type-ref/type-def/array/tuple/ownership/union/nullable/module/member-ref/assembly-ref nodes, and enforces that recursive counts consume exactly the payload with no trailing bytes. RED was the zrp metadata format test linking against the missing validator API. GREEN passes WSL gcc and WSL clang `zr_vm_zrp_metadata_format_test` 11/0 plus filtered metadata CTest 3/3 on both toolchains; the Windows MSVC CLI smoke still prints `hello world`. This is structural validation only; token/type/string semantic resolution, compiler signature-pool export, file-level zrp manifest read/write, and dump/diff tooling remain open.

Focused 2026-06-24 11-S7A zrp project manifest normalization gates closes the first loader-level `.zrp` manifest slice from the assembly-config design. `ZrLibrary_Project_New()` now rejects unsupported `manifestVersion` values instead of silently treating future schema versions as v1, and duplicate dependency refs are idempotent only when old `dependencies.$alias` and new `references.alias` normalize to the same package, assembly name, and version range. RED was the new `zr_vm_project_manifest_normalization_test` failing because an identical mixed old/new reference was rejected and `manifestVersion: 2` was accepted. GREEN passes WSL gcc and WSL clang `zr_vm_project_manifest_normalization_test` 3/0 plus `zr_vm_project_import_resolver_test` 9/0 on both toolchains; the Windows MSVC CLI smoke still prints `hello world`. This is only loader normalization; preserve-rule parsing, symbol/token retention, AOT mode, default-minimal metadata strategy, runtime binding diagnostics, and dump/diff tooling remain open.

Focused 2026-06-24 11-S7B zrp project manifest publicKeyToken normalization closes the next assembly identity text gate. `ZrLibrary_Project_New()` now treats `assembly.publicKeyToken` as hexadecimal identity text, lowercases `A-F` in the parsed manifest JSON before storing the project string, rejects non-hex token text, and preserves `null` as the no-token case. RED was the manifest normalization test accepting `not-hex` and preserving uppercase `A1B2...`. GREEN passes WSL gcc and WSL clang `zr_vm_project_manifest_normalization_test` 5/0 plus `zr_vm_project_import_resolver_test` 9/0 on both toolchains; the Windows MSVC CLI smoke still prints `hello world`. This is identity text normalization only; strong-name validation, runtime binding diagnostics, preserve-rule parsing, default-minimal metadata strategy, and dump/diff tooling remain open.

Focused 2026-06-24 11-S7C zrp project manifest legacy identity/schema parity closes another Layer 1 manifest-normalization gate. `ZrLibrary_Project_New()` now validates compatibility top-level `name` through the same assembly-name shape rules used by `assembly.name`, rejects present-but-invalid legacy `name`/`version` JSON shapes, and keeps identity defaults locked at version `0.0.0`, culture `neutral`, kind `library`, and null public key token. `zrp.schema.json` now mirrors those v1 constraints for `manifestVersion`, legacy `name`, publicKeyToken hex/null, and `kind`. RED was the manifest normalization test accepting `name: "app render"`; GREEN passes WSL gcc and WSL clang `zr_vm_project_manifest_normalization_test` 8/0 plus `zr_vm_project_import_resolver_test` 9/0 on both toolchains, JSON schema syntax validation, and the Windows MSVC CLI smoke still prints `hello world`. This is identity/schema parity only; preserve-rule parsing, AOT mode, runtime binding diagnostics, default-minimal metadata strategy, and dump/diff tooling remain open.

Focused 2026-06-24 11-S7D zrp project manifest legacy declared assembly mapping closes the compatibility-mapping gate for old `dependencies.$alias` object declarations. `ZrLibrary_Project_New()` now accepts `assembly` or legacy `name` as the declared target assembly identity, rejects invalid or conflicting declarations, rejects target `.zrp` manifest identity mismatches, and keeps dotted assembly identities importable by retaining the dependency alias as the package key while storing the real assembly identity on package/ref metadata. `ZrLibrary_Project_GetDependencyImportVersionRange()` now exposes that real identity for later AssemblyRef metadata, and `zrp.schema.json` mirrors the old dependency `assembly`/`name` fields. RED was the manifest normalization test rejecting `assembly: "zr.math"` and accepting a `name: "math"` dependency whose target manifest declared `physics`; a refinement RED caught that the metadata query still returned a null assembly identity. GREEN passes WSL gcc and WSL clang `zr_vm_project_manifest_normalization_test` 10/0 plus `zr_vm_project_import_resolver_test` 9/0 on both toolchains, JSON schema syntax validation, and the Windows MSVC CLI smoke still prints `hello world`. This is legacy dependency declared-assembly normalization only; preserve-rule parsing, AOT mode, runtime binding diagnostics, default-minimal metadata strategy, dump/diff tooling, and a later manifest loader/resolver split remain open.

Focused 2026-06-24 12-S1A reachability validation adds the first independent code-stripping mark engine for AOT. `backend_aot_reachability.{h,c}` defines the `unmarked` / `marked_pending` / `processed` state machine, dependency reasons for roots, manifest preservation, direct calls, field access, virtual calls, reflection, and generic instances, plus edge and mark records that store the first reason and predecessor. `backend_aot_reachability_compute()` runs BFS over caller-provided buffers, so later function-table filtering can consume the result without introducing allocator ownership into the marking core. RED was the new `zr_vm_aot_reachability_test` failing after reconfiguration because `backend_aot_reachability.h` did not exist; GREEN passes reachability 2/0, CTest `aot_reachability` 1/1, and AOT source contracts 19/0. This is only 12-S1A: real SemIR/bytecode scanning, virtual/interface closure, generic-instance closure, function-table filtering, size statistics, and full-AOT closure diagnostics remain open.

Focused 2026-06-24 12-S2A function table reachability-filter validation adds the first sweep-side consumer for the AOT reachability marks without changing default generated C yet. `backend_aot_function_table.{h,c}` now exposes `backend_aot_filter_function_table_by_reachability()`, which compacts an existing `SZrAotFunctionTable` in place, skips `UNMARKED` entries, keeps reachable entries' original `flatIndex` values, and rejects inconsistent table or mark-array bounds. RED was the expanded `zr_vm_aot_reachability_test` linking against a missing filter symbol; GREEN passes reachability 3/0, CTest `aot_reachability` 1/1, and AOT source contracts 19/0. This is only 12-S2A: the default AOT C emitter still needs to consume the filtered table, prove dead functions are not emitted, and measure the resulting size reduction.

Focused 2026-06-24 12-S2B sparse AOT index-space validation removes the next blocker to real function-table filtering. `SZrAotFunctionTable` now records `indexSpace`, so filtering can compact reachable entries without shortening the original function-index address space that the runtime loader and direct-call metadata use. The C emitter now declares functions by `entry->flatIndex`, writes `zr_aot_function_thunks[]` and `zr_aot_method_infos[]` across `functionIndexSpace`, fills removed function holes with `ZR_NULL`, and publishes descriptor counts using that original index space instead of the compacted reachable count. RED was the new index-space contract linking against a missing helper, then the frame setup source contract missing sparse emitter text; GREEN passes reachability 3/0, frame setup contracts 1/0, source contracts 19/0, shared-library smoke 8/0, and CTest `aot_reachability` 1/1. This is still only a 12-S2 support slice: real root/export/manifest reachability input, default filtering, dead-function emission proof, and size statistics remain open.

Focused 2026-06-24 12-S2C static callable reachability-graph validation adds the first real bytecode graph input for AOT trimming without enabling default filtering yet. `backend_aot_reachability_function_graph.{h,c}` now roots the graph at function flat index 0, scans `GET_CONSTANT`, `CREATE_CLOSURE`, and `GET_SUB_FUNCTION` for statically resolvable callable targets, emits `DIRECT_CALL` reachability edges, and feeds those edges into the existing BFS mark engine. The focused reachability test hand-builds a root function with a `GET_SUB_FUNCTION` instruction, verifies the child function is marked with predecessor 0 while an unused function remains `UNMARKED`, and checks edge-buffer capacity rejection. RED was the missing `backend_aot_reachability_function_graph.h`; GREEN passes reachability 4/0, CTest `aot_reachability` 1/1, and source contracts 19/0. This remains a 12-S2 sub-slice: default C emitter filtering, export/manifest roots, dead-function emission proof, and size statistics remain open.

Focused 2026-06-24 12-S2D opt-in AOT C code-stripping validation wires the reachability result into generated C behind an explicit writer option. `SZrAotWriterOptions.enableCodeStripping` now lets `ZrParser_Writer_WriteAotCFileWithOptions()` call the static callable graph, filter the function table, and still keep the original sparse `indexSpace` for thunk and MethodInfo tables. The new `zr_vm_aot_c_code_stripping_test` hand-builds root + reachable child + unused child, enables stripping, and verifies generated C emits `zr_aot_fn_0` and `zr_aot_fn_1` but not `zr_aot_fn_2`, while both descriptor tables keep a `ZR_NULL` hole for index 2. RED was the missing writer option member; GREEN passes the code-stripping test 1/0, reachability 4/0, source contracts 19/0, shared-library smoke 8/0, and CTest `aot_c_code_stripping|aot_reachability` 2/2. This proves dead functions can be omitted from generated C in opt-in mode; default trimming, export/manifest roots, trim diagnostics, and size statistics remain open.

Focused 2026-06-24 12-S2E export callable roots validation closes the first safety gap in opt-in code stripping. `backend_aot_compute_static_callable_reachability()` now receives caller-owned root buffers, keeps flat index 0 as `ROOT_ENTRY`, and scans the entry function's `SZrFunctionTopLevelCallableBinding` records so exported function bindings with valid child indices become `ROOT_EXPORT` roots. The opt-in C emitter allocates and passes those root buffers before filtering. RED was the focused reachability test switching to the root-buffer API while the helper still had a fixed entry-only root list; GREEN passes reachability 5/0, code stripping 2/0, CTest `aot_c_code_stripping|aot_reachability` 2/2, source contracts 19/0, and shared-library smoke 8/0. This means an otherwise-unused child callable is still emitted when it is a module export, while ordinary unused children remain eligible for trimming; manifest roots, default trimming, diagnostics, and size statistics remain open.

Focused 2026-06-24 12-S4A manifest preserve function roots validation adds the first parsed-manifest input channel to the trimming graph. `SZrAotWriterOptions` now carries `manifestPreserveFunctionFlatIndices` plus `manifestPreserveFunctionFlatIndexCount`; the static callable reachability helper imports those roots with `ZR_AOT_REACHABILITY_REASON_MANIFEST`, rejects invalid root indices, and the opt-in C emitter passes the option through before filtering. RED was the reachability test requiring the manifest-root helper shape while the implementation only had entry/export roots. GREEN passes reachability 6/0, code stripping 3/0, CTest `aot_c_code_stripping|aot_reachability` 2/2, source contracts 19/0, and shared-library smoke 8/0. This proves an otherwise-unused function can be preserved by parsed manifest input; zrp manifest parsing, symbol/token matching, annotations, feature switches, and trim warnings remain open.

Focused 2026-06-24 11-S7E / 12-S4B zrp manifest preserve declaration parsing adds the missing project-manifest file layer in front of the existing manifest-root writer option. `zr_vm_library` now exposes `SZrLibrary_ProjectPreserveRule` plus `preserveRules`/`preserveRuleCount`, and `project_preserve.{h,c}` parses top-level `.zrp` `preserve` arrays with `type`, `method`, or `generic` targets plus optional `members` (`all`/`methods`). `zrp.schema.json` mirrors that declaration shape, and invalid target text is rejected during project load. RED was project manifest normalization failing to compile because the project model had no preserve fields/enums; GREEN passes WSL gcc/clang manifest normalization 12/0 and import resolver 9/0, JSON schema parsing, Windows MSVC manifest normalization 12/0 and import resolver 9/0, plus CLI `hello_world`. This is declaration parsing only: preserve targets are not yet mapped to metadata tokens, function flat indices, generic instantiations, writer roots, annotations, or feature switches.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S7F zrp manifest AOT mode declaration parsing adds the file-level policy surface referenced by 08 full-AOT planning. `zr_vm_library` now exposes `EZrLibrary_ProjectAotMode` and `SZrLibrary_Project.aotMode`, while `project_aot_options.{h,c}` parses top-level `.zrp` `aotMode` values. Missing mode defaults to `hybrid`, explicit `full-aot` records `ZR_LIBRARY_PROJECT_AOT_MODE_FULL_AOT`, and invalid values reject the manifest. `zrp.schema.json` mirrors the `hybrid`/`full-aot` enum. Focused 2026-06-25 11-S7G zrp manifest AOT mode writer injection adds the CLI/compiler bridge from the project model to AOT writer options. `ZrCli_Compiler_ApplyProjectAotWriterOptions()` maps `SZrLibrary_Project.aotMode` to `SZrAotWriterOptions.requireFullAot`, setting true for `full-aot` and false for the default hybrid path while preserving other writer options. Focused 2026-06-24 09-S1B AOT GC descriptor module-table validation closes the descriptor registration gap left by 09-S1A. The public AOT ABI is now version 6 and defines `SZrAotGcDescriptor`; `ZrAotCompiledModule` publishes `gcDescriptors` plus `gcDescriptorCount` so generated value-type GC descriptors are visible through the module descriptor instead of remaining private generated-C statics. `backend_aot_c_type_layouts.c` now emits `static const SZrAotGcDescriptor ZrGcDescriptor_<id>` and a sparse `zr_aot_gc_descriptors[]` table indexed by `typeLayoutId`, while POD/no-GC modules publish `ZR_NULL` and `0u`. This closes 09-S1's descriptor emission, scan-table, and module metadata registration surface; precise AOT stack roots, safepoints, write barriers, boxing/FFI pinning, and later runtime token/layout hydration remain separate 09/11 work.

Focused 2026-06-24 12-S7A function stripping statistics adds the first concrete size-statistics surface for opt-in AOT C code stripping. Generated C now records `code_stripping.enabled`, `code_stripping.functionsBefore`, `code_stripping.functionsAfter`, and `code_stripping.functionsRemoved` in the file header after reachability filtering. The existing code-stripping fixture reports 3 functions before filtering and 2 after filtering when an unused child is removed; the export-root and manifest-root variants report 3 before, 3 after, and 0 removed. Focused 2026-06-24 12-S7B emitted function body byte statistics extends the opt-in code-stripping statistics from counts to per-emitted-function generated-C spans. When code stripping is enabled, `backend_aot_c_emitter.c` records the output position before and after `backend_aot_write_c_function_body()` and appends `code_stripping.functionBodyBytes[flatIndex] = <bytes>` after each generated function body. Focused 2026-06-24 12-S7C retained function body byte total adds the first aggregate generated-C body statistic for opt-in AOT code stripping. The emitter now sums the per-function spans captured around `backend_aot_write_c_function_body()` and writes `code_stripping.functionBodyBytesTotal = <bytes>` after all retained function bodies are emitted. Trimmed functions are naturally excluded because the loop walks the filtered function table; export-root and manifest-root preserved functions contribute to the total. Focused 2026-06-24 12-S7D generated type-layout byte statistics extends size attribution from function bodies to generated value-type layout carriers. `backend_aot_c_type_layouts.c` now records the output span for each `ZrLayout_<typeLayoutId>` block and appends `aot_size.typeLayoutBytes[typeLayoutId] = <bytes>` after the layout typedef/static assertions and any colocated generated GC descriptor. Focused 2026-06-24 12-S7H type-layout trim before/after statistics adds the first type-layout side of opt-in code-stripping comparison. `backend_aot_c_type_layouts.{h,c}` now exposes `backend_aot_c_type_layout_count_referenced()` so `backend_aot_c_emitter.c` can write `code_stripping.typeLayoutsBefore`, `code_stripping.typeLayoutsAfter`, and `code_stripping.typeLayoutsRemoved` beside the existing function-count statistics. Focused 2026-06-27 12-S7ZG zrp MethodSpec signature-pool rewrite/compaction closes the next emitted-metadata pruning gap for retained signature blobs. `backend_aot_c_zrp_metadata_signature.{h,c}` now collects signature blob slices referenced by retained token records and retained definition rows, deduplicates exact slices, copies a compacted signature blob pool, remaps signature blob offsets, and recomputes stable signature hashes from the final emitted bytes. For retained MethodSpec rows whose instantiation signature has the current `GENERIC_INST(MEMBER_REF methodToken, args...)` shape, the signature payload's method token is rewritten through the same compacted `MEMBER_DEF` MethodDef token map used by MethodSpec rows before hashes are recomputed. RED was the MethodSpec direct zrp fixture failing 1/5 once it required signature pool 30->15, MethodSpec signature method-token RID 2->1, and token record / MethodSpec hash recomputation; GREEN passes zrp pruning 5/0, code stripping 5/0, source contracts 21/0, frame setup 1/0, typed scalar, shared-library smoke, and focused CTest across WSL gcc, WSL clang, and Windows MSVC Debug. Focused 2026-06-26 12-S7ZF zrp MethodSpec method-token cascade removes the next conservative emitted-metadata guard without claiming signature-pool compaction. `backend_aot_c_zrp_metadata_prune.c` now compacts the MethodSpec section while `backend_aot_c_zrp_metadata_remap.{h,c}` remaps each retained MethodSpec `methodToken` through the same shared `MEMBER_DEF` MethodDef/FieldDef remapper used by token records. MethodSpec rows pointing at removed MethodDefs are dropped; rows pointing at retained MethodDefs survive with compacted method tokens. The signature blob pool is preserved byte-for-byte in this slice, so retained MethodSpec `instantiationBlobOffset`, `instantiationBlobLength`, and `instantiationHash` remain valid until a later pool rewrite. Focused 2026-06-26 12-S7ZE zrp GenericParamConstraint cascade removes the next conservative emitted-metadata guard after GenericParam owner/range remapping. `backend_aot_c_zrp_metadata_prune.c` now copies a compacted GenericParamConstraint section, while `backend_aot_c_zrp_metadata_remap.{h,c}` maps constraint `genericParamIndex` values through the retained GenericParam table, counts retained constraints, and recomputes each retained GenericParam's `firstConstraintIndex` plus `constraintCount`. Focused 2026-06-26 12-S7ZB zrp FieldDef member-token remap removes the conservative FieldDef guard introduced by S7ZA. `backend_aot_c_zrp_metadata_prune.c` now treats MethodDef and FieldDef rows as a shared `MEMBER_DEF` RID space during emitted blob rebuild: retained MethodDefs keep compact RIDs first, FieldDefs follow the retained MethodDef count, FieldDef row tokens are rewritten, and token-record member fields that point at FieldDefs are remapped to the same compact tokens. Token records that still point at removed MethodDefs are dropped. Focused 2026-06-26 12-S7ZA zrp token-record MethodDef pruning extends the S7Z emitted metadata rewrite past MethodDef rows. `backend_aot_c_zrp_metadata_prune.c` now builds retained MethodDef token mappings, rewrites retained MethodDef rows to compact `MEMBER_DEF` RIDs, copies only token records whose member references still point at retained MethodDefs, and remaps those token-record member fields to the same compact tokens. Focused 2026-06-24 12-S7I/12-S7J runtime fallback trim warning markers add the first generated trim-warning surface for hybrid AOT C modules that retain dynamic runtime fallback. `backend_aot_c_runtime_fallback.{h,c}` now owns the full-AOT/runtime-fallback scan used to count and emit `trim_warnings.runtimeFallbackCount` plus `trim_warning.runtimeFallback[index] function=<flatIndex> instruction=<instructionIndex> sourceLine=<debugLine> reason=<kind>` comments before the descriptor size markers; `backend_aot_c_emitter.c` only calls that diagnostics boundary during file emission. Focused 2026-06-25 11-S7H / 08-S7 / 12-S8G CLI AOT C emission entry wires the project compiler surface to the AOT C writer. `--emit-aot-c` now flows through `SZrCliCommand.emitAotC`; project compilation resolves `bin/aot_c/src/<module>.c`, writes `.zro`, reads it as the binary embedded module blob, sets `SZrAotWriterOptions.inputKind = ZR_AOT_INPUT_KIND_BINARY`, applies `.zrp aotMode` through `ZrCli_Compiler_ApplyProjectAotWriterOptions()`, and emits the generated C file. Focused 2026-06-25 11-S7I / 12-S4C method preserve root binding closes the first real manifest preserve-to-trim-root bridge. `ZrParser_Writer_ResolveTopLevelCallableFlatIndex()` builds the AOT function table and resolves an entry function top-level callable binding name to its stable flat function index. `ZrCli_Compiler_ApplyProjectAotPreserveRules()` consumes current-module `.zrp` `preserve` rules with `kind: "method"` and injects those flat indices into `SZrAotWriterOptions.manifestPreserveFunctionFlatIndices` before `--emit-aot-c` calls the writer. GREEN passes WSL gcc, WSL clang, and Windows MSVC Debug focused CTest groups, and the generated C preserves `main.kept` as `zr_aot_fn_2` with code-stripping counts `3/3/0`. Type/generic preserve, metadata-token resolution, cross-module method targets, annotations, and feature switches remain later 11/12 work.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S7J / 12-S4D dotted and type-member preserve roots expands that bridge to the callable naming shapes used by member-style AOT exports. `method "Widget.kept"` now matches the exact dotted top-level callable binding name before any current-module prefix fallback, and `type "Widget" members methods/all` scans top-level callable bindings for the `Widget.` prefix and injects every matching method as a manifest root. RED was the new dotted method and type-members CLI writer options tests seeing zero resolved roots. GREEN passes WSL gcc, WSL clang, and Windows MSVC Debug focused CTest groups; generated C preserves the originally unreachable `Widget.kept` path and the `Widget.used`/`Widget.kept` prefix set with code-stripping counts `3/3/0`. Generic preserve roots, metadata-token resolution, cross-module targets, annotations, and feature switches remain later 11/12 work.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S7K / 12-S4E preserve feature condition model adds the manifest-side condition fields needed before feature-switch trimming can be evaluated. `SZrLibrary_ProjectPreserveRule` now stores `feature`, `hasFeatureValue`, and `featureValue`; `project_preserve.c` accepts safe dotted feature names paired with boolean expected values and rejects half-declared conditions. `zrp.schema.json` mirrors `feature` / `featureValue` and their mutual dependency. RED was the manifest normalization test failing to compile because the project preserve rule had no feature fields. GREEN passes WSL gcc, WSL clang, and Windows MSVC Debug `zr_vm_project_manifest_normalization_test` 17/0, schema JSON parsing, WSL gcc CTest `cli_aot_writer_options|aot_c_code_stripping` 2/2, and `git diff --check` with only LF/CRLF warnings. This is still only the declaration model; build configuration values are not yet consumed to turn preserve roots on or off.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S7L / 12-S4F feature switch preserve root gating connects those feature-conditioned preserve declarations to project build switches for the currently supported preserve-root shapes. `zr_vm_library` now parses top-level `.zrp` `features` boolean maps into `SZrLibrary_ProjectFeatureSwitch` records, rejects invalid switch names and non-boolean switch values, and frees the switch table with the project model. `zrp.schema.json` mirrors the safe dotted boolean map. `ZrCli_Compiler_ApplyProjectAotPreserveRules()` now evaluates each rule's `feature` / `featureValue` pair before resolving method or type-member roots, so a matching switch injects the writer manifest root and a mismatched or missing switch leaves the otherwise-unreachable function eligible for trimming. RED was manifest normalization and CLI writer-option tests failing to compile because the feature switch model and gating did not exist. GREEN passes WSL gcc, WSL clang, and Windows MSVC Debug `zr_vm_project_manifest_normalization_test` 19/0 and `zr_vm_cli_aot_writer_options_test` 5/0, WSL gcc CTest `cli_aot_writer_options|aot_c_code_stripping` 2/2, schema JSON parsing, and `git diff --check` with only LF/CRLF warnings. This covers current same-module method and type-member roots only; generic preserve roots, metadata-token resolution, cross-module targets, annotations, default-minimal metadata policy, and dump/diff tooling remain open.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S7M / 12-S4G generic preserve argument model gives generic preserve declarations a concrete type-argument carrier before they are bound into generic-instantiation roots. `SZrLibrary_ProjectPreserveRule` now stores `genericArguments`, `genericArgumentCount`, and `genericArgumentCapacity`; `project_preserve.c` requires `kind: "generic"` rules to provide a non-empty `arguments` array, validates each argument as a safe dotted type name, rejects missing/non-array/empty/invalid arguments, and rejects `arguments` on non-generic rules. `zrp.schema.json` mirrors the `arguments` array with `minItems: 1` and conditional generic-only constraints. RED first compiled against missing `genericArgumentCount` / `genericArguments`, then runtime REDs showed missing, empty, or non-generic argument arrays were accepted. GREEN passes WSL gcc, WSL clang, and Windows MSVC Debug `zr_vm_project_manifest_normalization_test` 25/0, schema JSON parsing, WSL gcc CTest `cli_aot_writer_options|aot_c_code_stripping` 2/2, and `git diff --check` with only LF/CRLF warnings. This is still declaration modeling only; MethodSpec/TypeSpec token binding, generic instantiation reachability roots, cross-module targets, annotations, and default-minimal metadata remain open.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S7N / 12-S4H / 08-S7C manifest generic preserve writer roots connects that generic preserve declaration model to the AOT C writer surface. `SZrAotWriterOptions` now carries `manifestPreserveGenericRoots` and `manifestPreserveGenericRootCount`; the CLI preserve bridge stores generic root target/argument text in `SZrCliAotPreserveRoots` and forwards it after feature gating. This is still a bridge only: it does not materialize MethodSpec/TypeSpec tokens, generic instantiation table records, cross-module generic targets, annotation roots, or default-minimal metadata output.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S7O / 12-S4I / 08-S7D manifest generic preserve TypeSpec binding takes the next narrow step from text roots to token identity. `SZrAotManifestGenericRoot` now includes optional TypeSpec/signature token and signature-hash fields; the CLI AOT preserve bridge scans current-function metadata records for a `TYPE_SPEC` whose signature blob is the current emitted `GENERIC_INST(TYPE_REF target, args...)` shape and matches the manifest generic target plus concrete arguments. When it matches, writer options carry the TypeSpec token, paired signature token, and hash, and generated C emits manifest diagnostics for all three values. RED was the CLI writer options test failing to compile when it asserted the missing token/hash fields. GREEN passes WSL gcc `zr_vm_cli_aot_writer_options_test` 7/0, plus WSL gcc, WSL clang, and Windows MSVC Debug CTest `cli_aot_writer_options|aot_c_code_stripping|aot_c_generic_call_typed|generic_instantiation|metadata_token_model` 5/5. This does not synthesize missing TypeSpec records, parse MethodSpec, materialize generic-instantiation reachability roots, bind cross-module generic targets, or close full-AOT missing-instance diagnostics.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S7P / 12-S8H / 08-S7E full-AOT manifest generic TypeSpec closure gate consumes that binding status in the writer. `ZrParser_Writer_WriteAotCFileWithOptions()` now checks manifest generic preserve roots before module/function table construction when `requireFullAot` is true; if any root lacks `hasTypeSpecBinding`, generation returns `ZR_FALSE`. Hybrid output remains unchanged and can still emit manifest diagnostics for text-only generic roots. This closes only the manifest generic preserve TypeSpec gate; MethodSpec parsing, TypeSpec synthesis, generic-instantiation table materialization, cross-module generic targets, annotation roots, and full mark-and-sweep closure diagnostics remain open.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S7Q / 12-S3A / 12-S4J / 08-S7F manifest generic TypeSpec-backed instantiation root turns bound manifest generic roots into a writer-visible generic instance identity. `SZrAotManifestGenericRoot` now carries `hasGenericInstantiationBinding`, `genericInstantiationBaseToken`, `genericInstantiationInstanceId`, and `genericInstantiationShareKind`; the CLI preserve bridge builds resolved type arguments from `.zrp` concrete argument text, reuses `SZrGenericInstantiationTable_GetOrAddResolved()`, and records the resulting base token, C instance id, and share kind.
