This is still TypeSpec-backed identity materialization only; open generic base tokens, MethodSpec parsing, TypeSpec synthesis, cross-module generic targets, annotation roots, and full mark-and-sweep generic closure remain open.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S7R / 12-S8I / 12-S3B / 08-S7G full-AOT generic instantiation closure gate consumes that instance identity in the writer closure check. `backend_aot_manifest_generic_roots_closed_for_full_aot()` now requires every full-AOT manifest generic preserve root to have both `hasTypeSpecBinding` and `hasGenericInstantiationBinding`; a root with TypeSpec/signature token metadata but no generic instance id/share kind returns `ZR_FALSE` before C emission. RED was the new CLI writer options test still accepting a TypeSpec-only generic root. GREEN passes WSL gcc `zr_vm_cli_aot_writer_options_test` 10/0, plus WSL gcc, WSL clang, and Windows MSVC Debug CTest `cli_aot_writer_options|aot_c_code_stripping|aot_c_generic_call_typed|generic_instantiation|metadata_token_model` 5/5. This is still a writer-side full-AOT gate only; open generic base tokens, MethodSpec parsing, TypeSpec synthesis, cross-module generic targets, annotation roots, reflection-driven generic construction, and full mark-and-sweep generic closure remain open.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S7S / 12-S3C / 12-S4K / 08-S7H generic instantiation open base token closes the current-module open-base identity gap left by the TypeSpec-backed materialization slice. `compiler_aot.c` now resolves a TypeSpec-bound manifest generic preserve root's generic instantiation base token by scanning current-function metadata token records for a matching `TYPE_REF` signature name; when present, `SZrGenericInstantiationTable_GetOrAddResolved()` receives the open generic `TYPE_REF` token, and when absent it falls back to the previous closed `TYPE_SPEC` token. RED was the new CLI writer options test constructing `TYPE_REF(List)` plus `TYPE_SPEC(List<Foo>)` and still receiving `0x07000001`; GREEN receives `0x05000001` and generated C reports that base token in the manifest diagnostics. Verification passes WSL gcc `zr_vm_cli_aot_writer_options_test` 11/0, plus WSL gcc, WSL clang, and Windows MSVC Debug CTest `cli_aot_writer_options|aot_c_code_stripping|aot_c_generic_call_typed|generic_instantiation|metadata_token_model` 5/5. MethodSpec parsing, TypeSpec synthesis, cross-module generic targets, annotation roots, reflection-driven generic construction, and full mark-and-sweep generic closure remain open.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S7T / 12-S3D / 12-S4L / 08-S7I generic instantiation TypeDef base token extends that identity path to current-module generic definitions. `compiler_aot.c` now accepts `GENERIC_INST(TYPE_DEF target, args...)` TypeSpec signatures when binding `.zrp` generic preserve roots, resolves the matching open generic `TYPE_DEF` record by target name, and passes that token to `SZrGenericInstantiationTable_GetOrAddResolved()`; `TYPE_REF` open-base behavior and the TypeSpec fallback remain intact. RED was the new CLI writer options test constructing `TYPE_DEF(List)` plus `TYPE_SPEC(List<Foo>)` failing to set `hasTypeSpecBinding`; GREEN binds the root, reports `genericInstance.baseToken = 0x02000001`, and keeps the full-AOT generic closure gates passing. Verification passes WSL gcc `zr_vm_cli_aot_writer_options_test` 12/0, plus WSL gcc, WSL clang, and Windows MSVC Debug CTest `cli_aot_writer_options|aot_c_code_stripping|aot_c_generic_call_typed|generic_instantiation|metadata_token_model` 5/5. MethodSpec parsing, TypeSpec synthesis, cross-module generic targets, annotation roots, reflection-driven generic construction, and full mark-and-sweep generic closure remain open.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S7U / 12-S3E / 12-S4M / 08-S7J manifest generic synthesized TypeSpec closes the current-module missing-TypeSpec gap for `.zrp` generic preserve roots. When a root such as `List<Foo>` has no existing closed `TYPE_SPEC`, `compiler_aot.c` now finds a same-name open `TYPE_DEF` or `TYPE_REF` metadata record, appends an in-memory writer-visible `TYPE_SPEC` plus paired `SIGNATURE` record/signature blob, and then materializes the generic instantiation identity through the existing open-base path. RED was the new full-AOT CLI writer options test with only `TYPE_REF(List)` metadata failing to set `hasTypeSpecBinding`; GREEN synthesizes TypeSpec token `0x07000001`, signature token `0x08000002`, open base token `0x05000001`, and generic instance id `1`. Verification passes WSL gcc `zr_vm_cli_aot_writer_options_test` 13/0, plus WSL gcc, WSL clang, and Windows MSVC Debug CTest `cli_aot_writer_options|aot_c_code_stripping|aot_c_generic_call_typed|generic_instantiation|metadata_token_model` 5/5. MethodSpec parsing, cross-module generic targets, annotation roots, reflection-driven generic construction, full `.zro` metadata persistence policy, and full mark-and-sweep generic closure remain open.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S7V / 12-S3F / 12-S4N / 08-S7K manifest generic MethodSpec binding adds the current-module generic method counterpart to the generic type root work. `SZrAotManifestGenericRoot` now carries MethodSpec token, method token, and instantiation signature hash; `compiler_aot.c` matches manifest generic targets such as `Factory.make<Foo>` to typed exported method metadata and existing `GENERIC_INST(MEMBER_REF methodToken, args...)` signatures; generated C reports the MethodSpec identity, and full-AOT accepts MethodSpec-bound generic method roots without requiring TypeSpec/generic type-instantiation identity. RED was the new CLI writer options test failing to compile because MethodSpec fields were absent; GREEN binds method-spec token `0x08000002`, method token `0x03000001`, and signature hash `0x2233445566778899`. Verification passes WSL gcc `zr_vm_cli_aot_writer_options_test` 14/0 plus WSL gcc, WSL clang, and Windows MSVC Debug CTest `cli_aot_writer_options|aot_c_code_stripping|aot_c_generic_call_typed|generic_instantiation|metadata_token_model` 5/5. Cross-module generic method targets, generic method body closure, zrp MethodSpec table persistence, annotation roots, reflection-driven generic construction, and full mark-and-sweep generic closure remain open.

Focused 2026-06-25 09-S2A AOT GC root map descriptor ABI publishes the first generated-C carrier for precise AOT stack roots without yet registering those roots with the runtime GC stack. `zr_aot_abi.h` now exposes `EZrAotGcRootLocationKind`, `SZrAotGcRootSlot`, and `SZrAotGcRootMap`; `backend_aot_c_method_metadata.c` resolves inline-struct frame slots through `ZrCore_Function_ResolvePrototypeFrameTypeLayout()` and emits `zr_aot_gc_root_slots_<flatIndex>[]` entries for every GC field offset in those layouts. Generated method info points `.gcRootMap` at the emitted map when roots exist and keeps `ZR_NULL` for POD/blittable or pure scalar bodies. The value-type shared-library smoke loads `ZrVm_GetAotCompiledModule()`, reads `methodInfos[0]->gcRootMap`, validates frame-byte-offset roots against the string-field struct descriptor, and confirms POD output has no root-map symbols. This closes only the ABI/publication portion of 09-S2; runtime root-stack push/pop, safepoint-driven GC, moving-GC pointer rewrite, write barriers, and pinning remain open.

Focused 2026-06-25 09-S2B runtime AOT root-frame stack completes the default frame-byte-offset path for precise AOT stack roots. `SZrState` now owns an AOT root-frame stack and the GC exposes `ZrCore_Gc_AotRootFramePush/Pop/Depth()` for generated prologue/epilogue registration. The GC mark path reads `SZrAotGcRootMap` slots from each registered frame and marks the `SZrTypeValue` at `frameBase + frameByteOffset`; the minor-GC rewrite path visits the same slots and rewrites forwarded object references in place. `ZrAotGeneratedModuleContext` now carries the resolved `SZrAotMethodInfo`, letting generated C push a root frame only when `methodInfo->gcRootMap` is non-null and emit no root-frame calls for POD/blittable output. The new core test proves push/pop balance and proves an AOT root above `stackTop` survives and rewrites during minor GC. This does not implement the optional local-address root location, safepoint insertion, write barriers, boxing, or FFI pinning.

Focused 2026-06-25 09-S3A safepoint insertion connects that precise-root path to controlled GC progress in generated C. Core GC now exposes `ZrCore_Gc_SafePoint(state)`, and the AOT C backend emits it after GC object/array allocation, after function calls, and before loop back-edge `goto` sites. Back-edge detection is deliberately syntactic and local (`targetInstructionIndex <= instructionIndex`) so forward control flow stays poll-free, preserving the pure straight-line scalar invariant. The generated-C smoke verifies the three marker classes (`allocation`, `call`, `back_edge`) in one function body and compiles the result on the Unix shared-library path; the core root-frame test now also proves a safepoint advances pending generational GC debt. This completes 09-S3A but does not add reference-field write barriers, boxing boundary changes, or FFI pinning.

Focused 2026-06-25 09-S4A public AOT write barrier API adds the first write-barrier boundary usable by generated and AOT runtime code. Core GC now exposes `ZrCore_Gc_WriteBarrier(state, ownerObject, value)` as the allowed AOT-facing entry point and delegates to the existing `ZrCore_Value_Barrier` remembered-set implementation. The AOT runtime closure/capture heap-owner value barrier paths now call that public GC boundary, while stack inline struct field stores remain barrier-free in generated C. The focused core test proves an old heap owner recording a young value enters the remembered set through the wrapper. This is a partial 09-S4 slice only: direct generated-C member/index heap-owner barrier insertion and compile-time elimination for provably new young owners remain 09-S4B work.

Focused 2026-06-25 09-S4B member/index heap-store barrier boundary closes the current generated-C member/index write path without duplicating barriers in generated code. Member, cached-member, dynamic index, and super-array writes lower to AOT runtime helpers, and those helpers delegate the actual heap store to the core object layer where the resolved target object is known. The core object store sites now use `ZrCore_Gc_WriteBarrier(state, ownerObject, value)` for key/value heap references instead of directly calling the lower-level value barrier, so the AOT path passes through the same public GC boundary while stack inline struct stores remain barrier-free. This still leaves the explicit compile-time elimination case for owners proven newly allocated in the current function as a later 09-S4C step.

Focused 2026-06-25 09-S4C new-owner write barrier elimination completes the planned 09-S4 path. The AOT C function-body dispatcher now performs a conservative backward proof for heap-store receiver slots: only a same-function `CREATE_OBJECT` / `CREATE_ARRAY` origin with no intervening call, control boundary, return, escape, or unknown slot use can select the no-barrier lowering. Those stores call `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_*NewOwnerNoWriteBarrier`, and the runtime delegates to core object APIs such as `ZrCore_Object_SetMemberAssumeNewOwnerNoWriteBarrier()` and `ZrCore_Object_SetByIndexAssumeNewOwnerNoWriteBarrier()`, which reuse existing object store logic with a `skipWriteBarrier` candidate flag. Core still rechecks the actual target object immediately before the store and skips the barrier only while that object remains `YOUNG_MOVABLE`; if an allocation safepoint or other GC progress has already promoted the owner, the same path falls back to the 09-S4B public `ZrCore_Gc_WriteBarrier` route. This closes 09's planned memory-management slices while leaving optional local-address roots, long GC stress, card-table optimization, and pinned-region demotion as later extensions.

Focused 2026-06-25 09-S5A public boxing/unboxing bridge boundary makes the existing typed↔dynamic conversion boundary explicit without changing conversion semantics. Core now exposes `ZrCore_Bridge_BoxTyped()` and `ZrCore_Bridge_UnboxTyped()` as the public AOT-facing bridge API, and those functions delegate to the existing execution `TO_OBJECT` / `TO_STRUCT` implementation. The AOT runtime helpers for generated `TO_OBJECT` and `TO_STRUCT` now call the bridge API, so generated C continues to box/unbox only at typed↔dynamic boundaries while direct execution conversion calls stay behind the bridge layer. This slice does not implement FFI pinning or change value-type allocation/layout behavior; pin/unpin remains the remaining 09-S5 work.

Focused 2026-06-25 09-S5B FFI native-call pin scope completes the current 09-S5 boundary work. Core now exposes `SZrGcNativeCallPin` plus `ZrCore_Gc_NativeCallPinObject/Value/Unpin()` so AOT/FFI code can create a temporary precise native-call root without exposing lower-level GC internals. The libffi symbol-call path pins self, owner, and GC argument values before entering native code, then releases those pins in cleanup; callback trampoline stack checks now restore the saved `stackTop` through `SZrFunctionStackAnchor` so callbacks that trigger GC or stack growth do not compare stale raw stack pointers. This keeps typed↔dynamic boxing behind the bridge from 09-S5A and keeps native-call pinning behind a GC API boundary, while leaving pinned-region demotion and unrelated FFI source-extern `pointer<T>` parsing as separate work.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S2A generated-C code registration carrier adds the first public code-registration surface planned by the zrp metadata work. The public AOT ABI is now version 8 and defines `SZrAotCodeRegistration`, carrying function pointers, MethodInfo pointers, reflection invoker buckets, GC descriptor pointers, and their counts. `ZrAotCompiledModule` now exposes `codeRegistration`; generated C emits `zr_aot_reflection_invokers[]` plus `zr_aot_code_registration`, while the legacy module fields continue pointing at the same arrays for compatibility. The shared-library smoke loads `ZrVm_GetAotCompiledModule()` and verifies the registration table matches the descriptor's function/method/GC fields and exposes the single current invoker bucket. Runtime descriptor validation now rejects missing `codeRegistration`, mismatched pointer/count tables, and missing invoker tables before dereference; descriptor diagnostics cover that path with 2/0 on WSL gcc/clang and 2 ignored Unix-only branches on MSVC. This is a carrier plus descriptor-safety slice only: module-load registration into `SZrMetadataRuntime`, token→function/layout lazy resolution, and the full token↔layout三向表 remain later 11-S2/11-S3/11-S4 work.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S2B runtime code registration context carrier consumes that generated code-registration surface from the runtime side. Loaded-module records now cache `codeRegistration`, `ZrAotGeneratedModuleContext` and `ZrAotGeneratedFrame` both carry the registration pointer, and runtime MethodInfo lookup plus callable constants, native direct calls, meta calls, and static direct calls use `record->codeRegistration->methodInfos/functionPointers` rather than reading legacy descriptor thunk fields. Generated C frame setup copies `zr_aot_context.codeRegistration` into the generated frame while retaining `functionThunks` as a compatibility view. RED was the frame setup contract failing on missing carrier/source text and then on record binding not appearing in pointer-record form; GREEN passes WSL gcc/clang frame setup 1/0, source contracts 19/0, shared-library smoke 8/0, descriptor diagnostics 2/0, and MSVC Debug frame/source 1/0 and 19/0 with the existing Unix-only shared-library/descriptor branches ignored. This still does not register modules into `SZrMetadataRuntime`, resolve token→function/layout, or build the token↔layout三向表.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S2C module metadata runtime registration carrier closes the first module-load registration step without claiming token resolution. Core now defines a minimal `SZrMetadataRuntime`, `SZrObjectModule` exposes attach/query APIs, and AOT module load registers the module, metadata function, `codeRegistration`, and table counts through `ZrCore_Module_AttachMetadataRuntime(record.module, record.moduleFunction, record.codeRegistration)`. GC mark/rewrite visits the metadata runtime's `metadataFunction`, so the carrier remains valid across collection. RED was `zr_vm_metadata_runtime_query_test` failing on the missing metadata-runtime header/API, then `zr_vm_aot_c_frame_setup_contracts_test` failing until the loader attach contract existed. GREEN passes WSL gcc/clang metadata runtime query 4/0, frame setup 1/0, source contracts 19/0, shared-library smoke 8/0, descriptor diagnostics 2/0, and MSVC Debug metadata/frame/source with Unix-only shared-library/descriptor branches ignored. Data metadata mmap attach, token→function/layout lazy resolution and caches, and the token↔layout三向表 remain later 11-S3/11-S4 work.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S3A metadata runtime method record lazy cache adds the first token lookup API on top of that carrier. `SZrMetadataRuntime` now has a single method-record cache, and `ZrCore_MetadataRuntime_ResolveMethodRecord()` resolves local `MEMBER_DEF` records from the attached metadata function's token table and imported `MEMBER_REF` records from the module metadata ref table. Null runtime, zero token, and non-method tokens are rejected, while a second lookup for the same token returns the cached record pointer. RED was `zr_vm_metadata_runtime_query_test` linking against the missing resolver; GREEN passes WSL gcc/clang metadata runtime query 5/0, frame setup 1/0, source contracts 19/0, shared-library smoke 8/0, descriptor diagnostics 2/0, and MSVC Debug metadata/frame/source with Unix-only shared-library/descriptor branches ignored. This is only method token record lazy/cache lookup; type/field resolve, data metadata mmap, signature semantic resolution, runtime entity materialization, and token↔layout mapping remain later work.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S3B metadata runtime type record lazy cache mirrors that first resolver for type tokens. `SZrMetadataRuntime` now has an independent type-record cache, and `ZrCore_MetadataRuntime_ResolveTypeRecord()` resolves local `TYPE_DEF` records from the attached metadata function's token table and imported `TYPE_REF` records from the module metadata ref table. Null runtime, zero token, and non-type tokens are rejected, while a repeated lookup returns the cached type record pointer. RED was `zr_vm_metadata_runtime_query_test` linking against the missing type resolver; GREEN passes WSL gcc/clang metadata runtime query 6/0, frame setup 1/0, source contracts 19/0, shared-library smoke 8/0, descriptor diagnostics 2/0, and MSVC Debug metadata/frame/source with Unix-only shared-library/descriptor branches ignored. Field resolve, TypeSpec, data metadata mmap, signature semantic resolution, runtime entity materialization, and token↔layout mapping remain later work.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S3C metadata runtime signature record lazy cache adds the paired-signature record lookup needed before later signature parsing. `SZrMetadataRuntime` now has an independent signature-record cache, and `ZrCore_MetadataRuntime_ResolveSignatureRecord()` resolves an entity token's related `SIGNATURE` record from local metadata records first, then from the module metadata ref table. Null runtime, zero token, and direct `SIGNATURE` token inputs are rejected, while a repeated lookup returns the cached signature record pointer. RED was `zr_vm_metadata_runtime_query_test` linking against the missing signature resolver; GREEN passes WSL gcc/clang metadata runtime query 7/0, frame setup 1/0, source contracts 19/0, shared-library smoke 8/0, descriptor diagnostics 2/0, and MSVC Debug metadata/frame/source with Unix-only shared-library/descriptor branches ignored. Field resolve, TypeSpec, data metadata mmap, signature blob semantic parsing, runtime entity materialization, and token↔layout mapping remain later work.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S3D metadata runtime TypeSpec type record cache closes the record-level TypeSpec gap without claiming semantic TypeSpec materialization. `ZrCore_MetadataRuntime_ResolveTypeRecord()` now treats `TYPE_SPEC` as a type-record token, resolves local TypeSpec records from the attached metadata function's token records, and reuses the existing type-record cache for repeated lookups. RED was `zr_vm_metadata_runtime_query_test` returning null for the new TypeSpec lazy/cache proof; GREEN passes WSL gcc/clang metadata runtime query 8/0, frame setup 1/0, source contracts 19/0, shared-library smoke 8/0, descriptor diagnostics 2/0, and MSVC Debug metadata/frame/source with Unix-only shared-library/descriptor branches ignored. Field resolve, data metadata mmap lookup, signature blob semantic parsing, TypeSpec/generic semantic binding, runtime entity materialization, and token↔layout mapping remain later work.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S3E metadata runtime field record lazy cache adds the field-side record resolver while staying below semantic FIELD_SIG parsing. `SZrMetadataRuntime` now has an independent field-record cache, and `ZrCore_MetadataRuntime_ResolveFieldRecord()` resolves field records from local `MEMBER_DEF` records or module `MEMBER_REF` records because current method and field definitions share the member token table. The field cache remains independent from the method cache, so a method lookup does not invalidate a cached field record. RED was `zr_vm_metadata_runtime_query_test` linking against the missing field resolver; GREEN passes WSL gcc/clang metadata runtime query 9/0, frame setup 1/0, source contracts 19/0, shared-library smoke 8/0, descriptor diagnostics 2/0, and MSVC Debug metadata/frame/source with Unix-only shared-library/descriptor branches ignored. FIELD_SIG parsing, method/field semantic discrimination, data metadata mmap lookup, runtime field entity materialization, and token↔layout mapping remain later work.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S3F metadata runtime zrp metadata mmap attach connects the runtime carrier to the raw data-metadata image without claiming row-level semantic resolution. `SZrMetadataRuntime` now stores the attached zrp metadata buffer, byte length, validated header copy, and `hasZrpMetadata` flag. `ZrCore_MetadataRuntime_AttachZrpMetadata()` rejects null/short/invalid buffers through the existing zrp header and definition-table validators, and `ZrCore_MetadataRuntime_GetZrpSectionView()` returns raw section views such as `typeDefs` from the runtime header. RED was `zr_vm_metadata_runtime_query_test` failing on the missing zrp attach/view fields and API; GREEN passes WSL gcc/clang metadata runtime query 10/0, frame setup 1/0, source contracts 19/0, shared-library smoke 8/0, descriptor diagnostics 2/0, and MSVC Debug metadata/frame/source with Unix-only shared-library/descriptor branches ignored. Row semantics, string/constant/signature pool interpretation, signature blob semantic parsing, runtime entity materialization, and token↔layout mapping remain later work.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S3G metadata runtime validated signature blob view links the existing signature-record resolver to the attached zrp signature blob pool. `ZrCore_MetadataRuntime_GetSignatureBlob()` now requires attached zrp metadata, resolves an entity token to its paired `SIGNATURE` record, reads the bounded pool slice, and reuses `ZrCore_ZrpMetadata_ValidateSignatureBlob()` so truncated or structurally invalid blobs fail with a cleared output view. RED was `zr_vm_metadata_runtime_query_test` linking against the missing API; GREEN passes WSL gcc/clang metadata runtime query 11/0, frame setup 1/0, source contracts 19/0, shared-library smoke 8/0, descriptor diagnostics 2/0, and MSVC Debug metadata/frame/source with Unix-only shared-library/descriptor branches ignored. This is still a validated byte-slice boundary only; signature AST construction, method/field/type signature semantic parsing, TypeSpec/generic binding, runtime entity materialization, and token↔layout mapping remain later work.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S3H metadata runtime method/field signature header view adds the first semantic read above the validated signature blob byte slice. `SZrMetadataRuntimeSignatureView` captures method/field root kind, method calling convention and flags, generic parameter count, method parameter count, return-type blob offset, parameter-list blob offset, and field-type blob offset. The reader skips nested type nodes only to locate the next header field; it does not materialize those nodes into type entities or bind TypeSpec/generic semantics. RED was `zr_vm_metadata_runtime_query_test` failing to compile on the missing view type/API; GREEN passes WSL gcc/clang metadata runtime query 12/0, frame setup 1/0, source contracts 19/0, shared-library smoke 8/0, descriptor diagnostics 2/0, and MSVC Debug metadata/frame/source with Unix-only shared-library/descriptor branches ignored. Nested signature AST construction, FIELD_SIG type entity parsing, TypeSpec/generic binding, runtime entity materialization, and token↔layout mapping remain later work.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S3I metadata runtime signature type-node view materializes the next byte-slice layer without binding runtime type entities. `SZrMetadataRuntimeSignatureTypeNodeView` records node kind, original blob offset, next blob offset, generic/base child offsets, child count, and raw payload values; `ZrCore_MetadataRuntime_ReadSignatureTypeNode()` reads those fields from validated signature blob slices for primitive, TYPE_REF/TYPE_DEF, and GENERIC_INST shapes while reusing the existing structural skip logic for nested ranges. RED was `zr_vm_metadata_runtime_query_test` failing to compile on the missing type-node view/API; GREEN passes WSL gcc/clang metadata runtime query 13/0, frame setup 1/0, source contracts 19/0, shared-library smoke 8/0, descriptor diagnostics 2/0, and MSVC Debug metadata/frame/source with Unix-only shared-library/descriptor branches ignored. TypeSpec/generic semantic binding, FIELD_SIG type entity parsing, runtime entity materialization, token↔layout mapping, and metadata policy remain later work.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S3J metadata runtime generic TypeSpec signature view closes the next TypeSpec layer without materializing runtime type entities. `SZrMetadataRuntimeTypeSpecSignatureView` and `ZrCore_MetadataRuntime_ReadTypeSpecSignatureView()` validate a local `TYPE_SPEC` token, its paired `SIGNATURE` record, the validated signature blob, a full-blob root `GENERIC_INST`, and a base `TYPE_REF` or `TYPE_DEF` node; the view exposes TypeSpec/signature identity, signature hash, the blob slice, generic root node, base node, argument count, and argument-list blob offset. RED was `zr_vm_metadata_runtime_query_test` failing to compile on the missing TypeSpec signature view/API; GREEN passes WSL gcc/clang metadata runtime query 14/0, frame setup 1/0, source contracts 19/0, shared-library smoke 8/0, descriptor diagnostics 2/0, and MSVC Debug metadata/frame/source with Unix-only shared-library/descriptor branches ignored. Generic semantic binding beyond the signature view, MethodSpec parsing, row-to-runtime entity materialization, token↔layout mapping, and metadata policy remain later work.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S3K metadata runtime generic TypeSpec base-token binding view adds the next binding layer while still staying below runtime type materialization. `SZrMetadataRuntimeTypeSpecGenericBindingView` and `ZrCore_MetadataRuntime_ReadTypeSpecGenericBindingView()` reuse the TypeSpec signature view, match the `GENERIC_INST` base `TYPE_REF` or `TYPE_DEF` node against existing type record signature blobs, and expose the resolved base token/base record. RED was `zr_vm_metadata_runtime_query_test` failing to compile on the missing base-token binding view/API; GREEN passes WSL gcc/clang metadata runtime query 16/0, frame setup 1/0, source contracts 19/0, shared-library smoke 8/0, descriptor diagnostics 2/0, and MSVC Debug metadata/frame/source with Unix-only shared-library/descriptor branches ignored. Generic argument semantic binding, MethodSpec runtime binding, row-to-runtime entity materialization, token↔layout mapping, and metadata policy remain later work.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S3L metadata runtime generic TypeSpec argument binding view adds indexed argument inspection without materializing runtime type entities. `SZrMetadataRuntimeTypeSpecGenericArgumentView` and `ZrCore_MetadataRuntime_ReadTypeSpecGenericArgumentView()` reuse the TypeSpec generic binding view, walk the `GENERIC_INST` argument list by index, expose the argument type-node view, and bind direct `TYPE_REF` or `TYPE_DEF` argument nodes to existing type record token/record pairs. RED was `zr_vm_metadata_runtime_query_test` failing to compile on the missing generic argument view/API; GREEN passes WSL gcc/clang metadata runtime query 17/0, frame setup 1/0, source contracts 19/0, shared-library smoke 8/0, descriptor diagnostics 2/0, and MSVC Debug metadata/frame/source with Unix-only shared-library/descriptor branches ignored. Nested/recursive argument binding, MethodSpec runtime binding, row-to-runtime entity materialization, token↔layout mapping, and metadata policy remain later work.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S3M metadata runtime MethodSpec signature view adds the first MethodSpec runtime signature read without changing token encoding. `SZrMetadataRuntimeMethodSpecSignatureView` and `ZrCore_MetadataRuntime_ReadMethodSpecSignatureView()` read a MethodSpec direct signature record from the `SIGNATURE` token table, validate `GENERIC_INST(MEMBER_REF methodToken, args...)`, and expose methodSpec token, method token/record, signature hash, method node, argument count, and argument-list blob offset. RED was `zr_vm_metadata_runtime_query_test` failing to compile on the missing MethodSpec view/API; GREEN passes WSL gcc/clang metadata runtime query 18/0, frame setup 1/0, source contracts 19/0, shared-library smoke 8/0, descriptor diagnostics 2/0, and MSVC Debug metadata/frame/source with Unix-only shared-library/descriptor branches ignored. Method instantiation materialization, generic dictionary binding, row-to-runtime entity materialization, token↔layout mapping, and metadata policy remain later work.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S4A metadata runtime TypeDef layout binding view starts the token↔cTypeId↔ZrLayout table from TypeDef-backed rows without claiming the full layout registry. `SZrMetadataRuntimeTypeDefLayoutBindingView` and `ZrCore_MetadataRuntime_ReadTypeDefLayoutBindingView()` bind a `TYPE_DEF` token to the existing type record, the attached zrp `TYPE_DEFS` row, `typeLayoutId`/`cTypeId`, layout version/hash, and a cached `SZrTypeLayout` pointer only when the metadata function's prototype layout cache already has a matching `cTypeId`. RED was `zr_vm_metadata_runtime_query_test` failing to compile on the missing TypeDef layout binding view/API; GREEN passes WSL gcc/clang metadata runtime query 19/0, frame setup 1/0, source contracts 19/0, shared-library smoke 8/0, descriptor diagnostics 2/0, and MSVC Debug metadata/frame/source with Unix-only shared-library/descriptor branches ignored. Code-registration layout registry emission, TypeSpec/generic layout materialization, runtime layout construction, reflection/generic/GC unified consumers, and full token/cTypeId/layout cache remain later work.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S4B code-registration type layout registry publishes the first generated-C layout table planned by the token↔cTypeId↔ZrLayout bridge. `ZR_VM_AOT_ABI_VERSION` is now 9, `SZrAotCodeRegistration` and `ZrAotCompiledModule` expose `typeLayouts/typeLayoutCount`, and the AOT C backend emits `SZrTypeLayoutField`, `SZrTypeLayout`, and sparse `zr_aot_type_layouts[]` entries for reachable inline struct layouts indexed by `typeLayoutId/cTypeId`. Runtime descriptor validation now rejects descriptor/codeRegistration registry mismatches and inconsistent null/count shapes. RED was `zr_vm_aot_c_source_contracts_test` failing on the missing public ABI field; GREEN passes WSL gcc/clang metadata runtime query 19/0, frame setup 1/0, source contracts 19/0, shared-library smoke 8/0, value-type shared-library smoke 2/0, descriptor diagnostics 2/0, and MSVC Debug metadata/frame/source/value-type with existing Unix-only branches ignored. TypeSpec/generic layout materialization, ownership offset emission, runtime layout construction, reflection/generic/GC unified consumers, and full token/cTypeId/layout cache remain later work.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S4C metadata runtime registry-backed TypeDef layout binding connects that generated-C registry back into the runtime metadata view. `ZrCore_MetadataRuntime_ReadTypeDefLayoutBindingView()` still exposes the TypeDef token, zrp TypeDef row, `typeLayoutId/cTypeId`, layout version, and layout hash, but the returned `SZrTypeLayout` now comes only from `runtime->codeRegistration->typeLayouts[typeLayoutId]` instead of the metadata function prototype layout cache. RED was `zr_vm_metadata_runtime_query_test` expecting the code-registration registry pointer and receiving the prototype layout pointer; GREEN passes WSL gcc/clang metadata runtime query 20/0, frame setup 1/0, source contracts 19/0, shared-library smoke 8/0, value-type shared-library smoke 2/0, descriptor diagnostics 2/0, and MSVC Debug metadata/frame/source/value-type with existing Unix-only branches ignored. TypeSpec/generic layout materialization, ownership offset emission, runtime layout construction, reflection/generic/GC unified consumers, and full token/cTypeId/layout cache remain later work.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S4D metadata runtime public type-layout resolver promotes that registry lookup to a reusable runtime API. `SZrMetadataRuntime` now mirrors `typeLayoutCount` when attached, `ZrCore_MetadataRuntime_ResolveTypeLayout()` resolves `typeLayoutId` through the code-registration layout registry with cTypeId validation, and the TypeDef layout binding view reuses that resolver. The new focused `zr_vm_metadata_runtime_type_layout_test` keeps this coverage outside the already large query test and proves null/NONE/out-of-range/sparse/mismatched cases plus no fallback to the prototype layout cache. GREEN passes WSL gcc/clang type-layout runtime 3/0, metadata runtime query 20/0, frame setup 1/0, source contracts 19/0, shared-library smoke 8/0, value-type shared-library smoke 2/0, descriptor diagnostics 2/0, and MSVC Debug with existing Unix-only branches ignored. TypeSpec/generic layout materialization, ownership offset emission, runtime layout construction, reflection/generic/GC unified consumers, and full token/cTypeId/layout cache remain later work.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S4E generic dictionary type-layout resolver connects the 08-S4 dictionary consumer to the same metadata runtime layout table. `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_GenericSlot_TypeLayout()` and `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_GenericSlot_TryGetSizeOf()` now receive `SZrMetadataRuntime*` and resolve TYPE_LAYOUT/SIZEOF via `ZrCore_MetadataRuntime_ResolveTypeLayout()` instead of using `metadataFunction->prototypeFrameTypeLayouts`; generated shared-reference generic code now passes `metadataRuntime` through `ZrAot_GenericSlot_TypeLayout(metadataRuntime, dict, slotIndex)`. RED proved a dictionary typeLayoutId with a stale prototype cache did not return the code-registration registry layout; GREEN returns the registry layout/size and rejects missing registry without fallback. WSL gcc/clang pass reference sharing 4/0, generic call typed 6/0, source contracts 19/0, frame setup 1/0, metadata type-layout 3/0, metadata query 20/0, shared-library smoke 8/0, value-type shared-library smoke 2/0, and descriptor diagnostics 2/0. MSVC Debug passes the same focused set with existing Unix-only shared-library branches ignored. This hardens the 08 dictionary layout consumer but does not close TypeSpec materialization, runtime layout construction, reflection/GC consumer migration, or full-AOT generic closure.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S4F GC descriptor metadata-runtime resolver adds the descriptor-side counterpart to that shared layout table. `ZrCore_MetadataRuntime_ResolveGcDescriptor()` now looks up `codeRegistration->gcDescriptors[typeLayoutId]` through `SZrMetadataRuntime`, requires `descriptor->typeLayoutId` to match the requested id, and refuses to return a descriptor unless the same id resolves through `ZrCore_MetadataRuntime_ResolveTypeLayout()` to the code-registration layout registry. The focused metadata type-layout test now proves valid descriptor lookup, sparse/mismatched/null rejection, and no fallback through stale `metadataFunction->prototypeFrameTypeLayouts`. RED was the focused test failing to compile/link on the missing resolver; GREEN passes WSL gcc/clang metadata type-layout 5/0, metadata query 20/0, AOT GC root-frame 5/0, frame setup 1/0, source contracts 19/0, value-type smoke 2/0, shared-library smoke 8/0, descriptor diagnostics 2/0, and generic reference sharing 4/0. MSVC Debug passes the same focused set, with only existing Unix-only shared-library branches ignored. This closes the public code-registration GC descriptor lookup entry but does not migrate GC inline-frame scanning, build TypeSpec/generic layouts, construct runtime layouts, or close reflection consumer migration.

Focused 2026-06-25 11-S4G GC inline-frame metadata-runtime layout resolver migrates the GC mark/rewrite consumer side of that table. AOT-loaded functions now attach the static code-registration layout registry to each `SZrFunction`, and `ZrCore_MetadataRuntime_ResolveFunctionTypeLayout()` resolves inline-frame `typeLayoutId` from the function or its prototype-context entry function registry. GC inline-frame mark/rewrite uses that resolver for attached AOT functions and refuses stale prototype fallback when a registry is present, while unbound VM/interpreter functions still use `ZrCore_Function_ResolvePrototypeFrameTypeLayout()` so ordinary inline-frame GC scanning remains intact. RED first caught the missing attach/resolve API in the focused metadata type-layout test, then caught the lost non-AOT fallback in `zr_vm_gc_test` when inline-frame minor rewrite work dropped from 2 to 1. GREEN passes WSL gcc/clang/MSVC Debug metadata type-layout 7/0, metadata query 20/0, AOT GC root-frame 5/0, GC 66/0, value-type runtime 14/0, frame/source/AOT smoke, descriptor diagnostics, and generic reference sharing. This closes GC inline-frame consumer migration to the runtime layout table but still leaves TypeSpec/generic layout materialization, runtime layout construction, reflection consumer migration, and the complete token/cTypeId/layout cache open.
